UTM Zone Auto-Detection
To auto-detect the UTM zone, I’ll implement a function to calculate the UTM zone from the longitude of the survey area’s centroid, as UTM zones are defined by 6-degree longitude bands (e.g., Zone 17 covers -84° to -78°). This will replace hardcoded EPSG codes (e.g., EPSG:32614, EPSG:32617) in area_utils.py, dsm_manager.py, and dem_downloader.py. The function will:

Use the centroid of the input coordinates (from shapely.geometry.Polygon).
Determine the UTM zone using the formula: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Set the EPSG code as 32600 + zone for Northern Hemisphere (since the log’s latitudes ~39°N are in the Northern Hemisphere).

utils.py (Reference)
Purpose: Shared utilities, including UTM zone auto-detection.
Code:

python
import logging
from shapely.geometry import Polygon
import math

# Configure logging
logging.basicConfig(
    filename="uas_survey_tool.log",
    level=logging.DEBUG,
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"
)

def get_utm_zone(coordinates):
    """
    Auto-detect UTM zone from coordinates.
    
    Args:
        coordinates (list): List of (lon, lat) tuples.
    
    Returns:
        str: EPSG code (e.g., 'EPSG:32617' for UTM Zone 17N).
    """
    try:
        if not coordinates or len(coordinates) < 3:
            raise ValueError("At least 3 coordinates required for UTM zone detection")

        polygon = Polygon(coordinates)
        centroid = polygon.centroid
        lon = centroid.x
        zone = math.floor((lon + 180) / 6) + 1
        hemisphere = "N" if centroid.y >= 0 else "S"
        epsg_code = f"EPSG:{32600 + zone}" if hemisphere == "N" else f"EPSG:{32700 + zone}"
        logging.debug(f"Auto-detected UTM zone: {epsg_code} (lon={lon:.2f}, lat={centroid.y:.2f})")
        return epsg_code
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"UTM zone detection failed: {e}")
        raise
1. main.py
Purpose: Entry point, initializes the PyQt6 application, validates the license key, and launches UASWindow.
Issues:

Uses print alongside logging, inconsistent with log format.
Hardcodes Fusion style; should use styles.qss.

Revised Code:

python
import sys
import logging
import os
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QApplication
from PyQt6.QtGui import QIcon
from modern_ui import UASWindow
from license_check import prompt_license_key

# Configure logging
log_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'logs')
os.makedirs(log_dir, exist_ok=True)
log_file = os.path.join(log_dir, 'uas_survey_tool.log')
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.DEBUG,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler(log_file, encoding='utf-8'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)

def main():
    """Main entry point for the UAS Survey Tool."""
    try:
        logging.debug("Starting application...")
        if not prompt_license_key():
            logging.error("License key validation failed. Exiting.")
            sys.exit(1)

        app = QApplication(sys.argv)
        # Load stylesheet
        try:
            with open(os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'styles.qss'), 'r') as f:
                app.setStyleSheet(f.read())
            logging.debug("Stylesheet loaded successfully.")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logging.warning("styles.qss not found. Using default styling.")

        # Set application icon
        icon_path = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'app_icon.ico')
        if os.path.exists(icon_path):
            app.setWindowIcon(QIcon(icon_path))
        else:
            logging.warning("app_icon.ico not found. Using default icon.")

        window = UASWindow()
        window.show()
        logging.debug("Application window shown. Starting event loop.")
        sys.exit(app.exec())
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Application error: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
Revisions:

Removed print statements, using logging only.
Loaded styles.qss instead of hardcoding Fusion style.
Added error handling for missing app_icon.ico.
Ensured log directory creation and UTF-8 encoding.

def resource_path(relative_path):
    """Get absolute path to resource, works for dev and PyInstaller."""
    base_path = getattr(sys, '_MEIPASS', os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
    return os.path.join(base_path, relative_path)

class TextEditHandler(logging.Handler):
    """Custom logging handler to output to QTextEdit."""
    def __init__(self, text_edit):
        super().__init__()
        self.text_edit = text_edit

    def emit(self, record):
        msg = self.format(record).encode('utf-8', errors='replace').decode('utf-8')
        self.text_edit.append(msg)
        self.text_edit.ensureCursorVisible()

class PointEditorDialog(QDialog):
    def __init__(self, gcp_points, verification_points, rejected_gcp_points, rejected_verification_points, polygon_coords, utm_crs, main_logic, dem_path=None, dsm_path=None, parent=None):

        self.setWindowTitle("Point Editor")
        self.gcp_points = gcp_points

        self.rejected_gcp_points = rejected_gcp_points
        self.rejected_verification_points = rejected_verification_points
        self.polygon_coords = polygon_coords
        self.utm_crs = utm_crs
        self.main_logic = main_logic
        self.dem_path = dem_path
        self.dsm_path = dsm_path
        self.selected_points = {
            'gcp': set(range(len(gcp_points))),
            'ver': set(range(len(verification_points))),
            'rejected_gcp': set(),
            'rejected_ver': set()
        }
        self.dragging = None
        self.drag_index = None
        self.drag_type = None
        self.gcp_counter = len(gcp_points) + 1
        self.ver_counter = len(verification_points) + 1
        self.reintroduction_history = []
        logging.debug(f"PointEditorDialog initialized with {len(gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(verification_points)} VCPs, "
                     f"{len(rejected_gcp_points)} rejected GCPs, {len(rejected_verification_points)} rejected VCPs")
        self.init_ui()

    def init_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout()
        self.setLayout(layout)
        self.setMinimumSize(800, 600)

        # Canvas for point visualization
        self.fig = Figure(figsize=(8, 6))
        self.canvas = FigureCanvas(self.fig)
        self.ax = self.fig.add_subplot(111)
        layout.addWidget(self.canvas)

        # Lists for point management in a scrollable area
        scroll_area = QScrollArea()
        scroll_area.setWidgetResizable(True)
        scroll_widget = QWidget()
        scroll_layout = QHBoxLayout(scroll_widget)
        scroll_layout.setContentsMargins(10, 10, 10, 10)
        scroll_layout.setSpacing(10)

        self.gcp_list = QListWidget()
        self.ver_list = QListWidget()
        self.rejected_gcp_list = QListWidget()
        self.rejected_ver_list = QListWidget()

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_ver_list.addItem(item)

        scroll_layout.addWidget(QLabel("GCPs:"))
        scroll_layout.addWidget(self.gcp_list)
        scroll_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Verification Points:"))
        scroll_layout.addWidget(self.ver_list)
        scroll_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Rejected GCPs:"))
        scroll_layout.addWidget(self.rejected_gcp_list)
        scroll_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Rejected Verification Points:"))
        scroll_layout.addWidget(self.rejected_ver_list)
        scroll_area.setWidget(scroll_widget)
        scroll_area.setStyleSheet("QScrollArea { border: none; background-color: #1e2a44; } "
                                 "QScrollBar:vertical { width: 12px; background: #2a3f73; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::handle:vertical { background: #3f5ca8; border-radius: 6px; min-height: 20px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::add-line:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-line:vertical { height: 0px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::add-page:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-page:vertical { background: none; }")
        layout.addWidget(scroll_area)

        self.gcp_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)
        self.ver_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)
        self.rejected_gcp_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)
        self.rejected_ver_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)

        self.canvas.mpl_connect('button_press_event', self.on_click)
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('motion_notify_event', self.on_motion)
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('button_release_event', self.on_release)
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('button_press_event', self.on_double_click)

        # Button layout
        button_widget = QWidget()
        button_layout = QHBoxLayout(button_widget)
        button_layout.setContentsMargins(10, 10, 10, 10)
        self.reintroduce_button = QPushButton("Reintroduce Selected")
        self.reintroduce_button.clicked.connect(self.reintroduce_selected)
        self.undo_button = QPushButton("Undo Last Reintroduction")
        self.undo_button.clicked.connect(self.undo_reintroduction)
        self.undo_button.setEnabled(False)
        button_layout.addWidget(self.reintroduce_button)
        button_layout.addStretch()
        button_layout.addWidget(self.undo_button)
        layout.addWidget(button_widget)

        # Dialog buttons
        buttons = QDialogButtonBox(QDialogButtonBox.StandardButton.Ok | QDialogButtonBox.StandardButton.Cancel)
        buttons.accepted.connect(self.accept)
        buttons.rejected.connect(self.reject)
        layout.addWidget(buttons)

        self.plot_points()

    def plot_points(self):
        self.ax.clear()
        try:
            if self.polygon_coords:
                if isinstance(self.polygon_coords[0], dict):
                    x_poly, y_poly = zip(*[(pt['easting'], pt['northing']) for pt in self.polygon_coords])
                else:
                    x_poly, y_poly = zip(*self.polygon_coords)
                self.ax.plot(x_poly + (x_poly[0],), y_poly + (y_poly[0],), 'k-', label="Polygon")
            else:
                logging.warning("No polygon coordinates to plot")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Failed to plot polygon: {e}")

        gcp_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        gcp_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        ver_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        ver_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        rej_gcp_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']]
        rej_gcp_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']]
        rej_ver_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']]
        rej_ver_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']]

        self.gcp_plot = self.ax.scatter(gcp_x, gcp_y, c='blue', marker='o', label="GCPs", alpha=1.0)
        self.ver_plot = self.ax.scatter(ver_x, ver_y, c='red', marker='x', label="Verification Points", alpha=1.0)
        self.rej_gcp_plot = self.ax.scatter(rej_gcp_x, rej_gcp_y, c='red', marker='o', label="Rejected GCPs", alpha=0.3)
        self.rej_ver_plot = self.ax.scatter(rej_ver_x, rej_ver_y, c='orange', marker='x', label="Rejected Verification Points", alpha=0.3)

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['gcp']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['elevation']:.2f}m)", fontsize=8, ha='right', va='bottom')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['ver']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['elevation']:.2f}m)", fontsize=8, ha='left', va='bottom')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['reason']})", fontsize=8, ha='right', va='bottom', color='gray')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['reason']})", fontsize=8, ha='left', va='bottom', color='gray')

        self.ax.legend(loc='upper right', bbox_to_anchor=(1.15, 1))
        self.ax.set_xlabel("Easting (m)")
        self.ax.set_ylabel("Northing (m)")
        self.ax.set_aspect('equal')
        self.canvas.draw()

    def on_click(self, event):
        if event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        min_dist = float('inf')
        closest_idx = None
        closest_type = None

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'gcp'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'ver'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'rejected_gcp'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                achievable_idx = i
                closest_type = 'rejected_ver'

        if closest_idx is not None:
            if event.button == 1 and not event.dblclick:
                if closest_type in ['gcp', 'ver']:
                    self.dragging = True
                    self.drag_index = closest_idx
                    self.drag_type = closest_type
            elif event.button == 3:
                if closest_type in ['gcp', 'ver', 'rejected_gcp', 'rejected_ver']:
                    item = (
                        self.gcp_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'gcp' else
                        self.ver_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'ver' else
                        self.rejected_gcp_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'rejected_gcp' else
                        self.rejected_ver_list.item(closest_idx)
                    )
                    item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Unchecked if item.checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked else Qt.CheckState.Checked)
                    self.update_selection()
            elif event.button == 1 and event.dblclick and closest_type in ['rejected_gcp', 'rejected_ver']:
                point = self.rejected_gcp_points[closest_idx] if closest_type == 'rejected_gcp' else self.rejected_verification_points[closest_idx]
                if QMessageBox.question(self, "Reintroduce Point", f"Reintroduce {point['name']} ({point['reason']})?") == QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:
                    self.reintroduce_point(closest_idx, closest_type)

    def on_double_click(self, event):
        if event.inaxes != self.ax or event.button != 1 or not event.dblclick:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        logging.debug(f"Double-click detected at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        polygon = Polygon(self.polygon_coords)
        if not polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
            logging.warning(f"New point at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}) is outside polygon")
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Invalid Location", "New point must be within the polygon boundary.")
            return

        point_type, ok = QInputDialog.getItem(self, "Add Point", "Select point type:", ["GCP", "Verification Point"], 0, False)
        if not ok:
            logging.debug("User cancelled point type selection")
            return

        transformer = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        lon, lat = transformer.transform(x, y)
        elevation = 0.0
        if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
            try:
                dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer)
                dem_dataset.close()
                if dsm_dataset:
                    dsm_dataset.close()
                if not suitable:
                    logging.warning(f"New point at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}) rejected: {reason}")
                    QMessageBox.warning(self, "Invalid Location", f"Cannot add point: {reason}")
                    return
                elevation = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Failed to sample elevation for new point: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", f"Failed to sample elevation: {e}")
                return

        if point_type == "GCP":
            name = f"GCP_new_{self.gcp_counter}"
            self.gcp_points.append({
                'lat': lat, 'lon': lon, 'name': name, 'elevation': elevation,
                'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': 0.0, 'global_offset': 0.0,
                'status': 'accepted', 'reason': '', 'type': 'GCP'
            })
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{name} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {elevation:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].add(len(self.gcp_points) - 1)
            self.gcp_counter += 1
            logging.info(f"Added new GCP: {name} at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        else:
            name = f"Veri_new_{self.ver_counter}"
            self.verification_points.append({
                'lat': lat, 'lon': lon, 'name': name, 'elevation': elevation,
                'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': 0.0, 'global_offset': 0.0,
                'status': 'accepted', 'reason': '', 'type': 'VCP'
            })
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{name} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {elevation:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['ver'].add(len(self.verification_points) - 1)
            self.ver_counter += 1
            logging.info(f"Added new Verification Point: {name} at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        self.plot_points()

    def reintroduce_point(self, index, point_type):
        if point_type == 'rejected_gcp':
            point = self.rejected_gcp_points.pop(index)
            point['status'] = 'accepted'
            point['manually_restored'] = True
            point['original_reason'] = point.get('reason', 'Unknown')
            point['reason'] = ''
            self.gcp_points.append(point)
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{point['name']} ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {point['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].add(len(self.gcp_points) - 1)
            self.reintroduction_history.append(('gcp', index, point))
            logging.info(f"Reintroduced GCP: {point['name']} at ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f})")
        else:
            point = self.rejected_verification_points.pop(index)
            point['status'] = 'accepted'
            point['manually_restored'] = True
            point['original_reason'] = point.get('reason', 'Unknown')
            point['reason'] = ''
            self.verification_points.append(point)
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{point['name']} ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {point['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['ver'].add(len(self.verification_points) - 1)
            self.reintroduction_history.append(('ver', index, point))
            logging.info(f"Reintroduced Verification Point: {point['name']} at ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f})")
        self.rejected_gcp_list.clear()
        self.rejected_ver_list.clear()
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_ver_list.addItem(item)
        self.undo_button.setEnabled(True)
        self.plot_points()

    def reintroduce_selected(self):
        selected_gcp = [i for i in range(self.rejected_gcp_list.count()) if self.rejected_gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked]
        selected_ver = [i for i in range(self.rejected_ver_list.count()) if self.rejected_ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked]
        for i in reversed(selected_gcp):
            self.reintroduce_point(i, 'rejected_gcp')
        for i in reversed(selected_ver):
            self.reintroduce_point(i, 'rejected_ver')
        self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'].clear()
        self.selected_points['rejected_ver'].clear()

    def undo_reintroduction(self):
        if not self.reintroduction_history:
            return
        point_type, index, point = self.reintroduction_history.pop()
        if point_type == 'gcp':
            self.gcp_points.remove(point)
            point['status'] = 'rejected'
            point['manually_restored'] = False
            point['reason'] = point['original_reason']
            self.rejected_gcp_points.append(point)
            self.gcp_list.takeItem(self.gcp_list.count() - 1)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].discard(len(self.gcp_points))
        else:
            self.verification_points.remove(point)
            point['status'] = 'rejected'
            point['manually_restored'] = False
            point['reason'] = point['original_reason']
            self.rejected_verification_points.append(point)
            self.ver_list.takeItem(self.ver_list.count() - 1)
            self.selected_points['ver'].discard(len(self.verification_points))
        self.rejected_gcp_list.clear()
        self.rejected_ver_list.clear()
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_ver_list.addItem(item)
        self.undo_button.setEnabled(bool(self.reintroduction_history))
        logging.info(f"Undid reintroduction of {point['name']}")
        self.plot_points()

    def on_motion(self, event):
        if not self.dragging or event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        polygon = Polygon(self.polygon_coords)
        if not polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
            return
        if self.drag_type == 'gcp':
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True).transform(x, y)
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            elevation = 0.0
            if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
                try:
                    dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                    dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                    suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True))
                    dem_dataset.close()
                    if dsm_dataset:
                        dsm_dataset.close()
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['elevation'] = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['status'] = 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected'
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['reason'] = reason
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Failed to update elevation for dragged point: {e}")
            self.gcp_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['elevation']:.2f}m)")
        elif self.drag_type == 'ver':
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True).transform(x, y)
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            elevation = 0.0
            if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
                try:
                    dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                    dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                    suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True))
                    dem_dataset.close()
                    if dsm_dataset:
                        dsm_dataset.close()
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['elevation'] = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['status'] = 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected'
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['reason'] = reason
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Failed to update elevation for dragged point: {e}")
            self.ver_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['elevation']:.2f}m)")
        self.plot_points()

    def on_release(self, event):
        self.dragging = False
        self.drag_index = None
        self.drag_type = None

    def update_selection(self):
        self.selected_points['gcp'] = {i for i in range(self.gcp_list.count()) if self.gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['ver'] = {i for i in range(self.ver_list.count()) if self.ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] = {i for i in range(self.rejected_gcp_list.count()) if self.rejected_gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] = {i for i in range(self.rejected_ver_list.count()) if self.rejected_ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.plot_points()

    def get_selected_points(self):
        selected_gcp = [self.gcp_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        selected_ver = [self.verification_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        return selected_gcp, selected_ver

class UASWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("UAS Survey Tool v2.0")
        icon_path = resource_path("app_icon.ico")
        self.setWindowIcon(QIcon(icon_path))
        self.main_logic = MainLogic()
        self.gcp_points = []
        self.verification_points = []
        self.rejected_gcp_points = []
        self.rejected_verification_points = []
        self.flight_params = {}
        self.area_name = ""
        self.polygon_coords = []
        self.elevation_data = {}
        self.diagnostic_report = ""
        self.kmz_loaded = False
        self.last_kmz_load_time = 0
        self.debounce_interval = 1.0
        self.init_ui()
        self.setup_logging()
        logging.debug("UASWindow instance created")
        result = self.main_logic.run_core_analysis()
        logging.debug(f"Core analysis result: {result}")

    def setup_logging(self):
        logging.getLogger().handlers = []
        logging.getLogger(__name__).handlers = []
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s", encoding='utf-8')
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        self.logger.propagate = False
        console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        console_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        console_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(console_handler)
        log_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'logs')
        os.makedirs(log_dir, exist_ok=True)
        log_path = os.path.join(log_dir, "uas_survey_tool.log")
        file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_path, encoding='utf-8')
        file_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        file_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(file_handler)
        handler = TextEditHandler(self.status_log)
        handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(handler)
        self.logger.debug(f"Logger handlers after setup: {len(self.logger.handlers)}")

    def init_ui(self):
        screen = QApplication.primaryScreen()
        screen_size = screen.availableGeometry()
        screen_width = screen_size.width()
        screen_height = screen_size.height()

        min_height = max(600, int(screen_height * 0.7))
        max_width = min(1400, int(screen_width * 0.9))
        max_height = min(1000, int(screen_height * 0.9))
        self.setMinimumSize(min_width, min_height)
        self.setMaximumSize(max_width, max_height)
        self.resize(min_width, 800)
        logging.debug(f"Screen size: {screen_width}x{screen_height}, Min size: {min_width}x{min_height}, Max size: {max_width}x{max_height}")

        scroll_area = QScrollArea()
        scroll_area.setWidgetResizable(True)
        scroll_area.setStyleSheet("QScrollArea { border: none; background-color: #1e2a44; } "
                                 "QScrollBar:vertical { border: none; background: #2a3f73; width: 10px; margin: 0px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::handle:vertical { background: #3f5ca8; border-radius: 5px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::add-line:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-line:vertical { background: none; }"

    def toggle_dem_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dem_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dem_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dem_input.setText("Auto-downloading DEM...")
        else:
            self.dem_input.clear()

    def toggle_dsm_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dsm_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dsm_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dsm_input.setText("Auto-downloading DSM...")
        else:
            self.dsm_input.clear()

    def browse_kmz(self):
        current_time = time.time()
        self.logger.debug(f"browse_kmz called at {current_time}")
        if current_time - self.last_kmz_load_time < self.debounce_interval:
            self.logger.debug("Debounced duplicate call to browse_kmz")
            return
        self.last_kmz_load_time = current_time
        self.kmz_loaded = False

        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select KMZ/KML File", "", "KMZ/KML Files (*.kmz *.kml)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.kmz_input.setText(file_path)
            self.area_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(file_path))[0].replace(" ", "_")
            kml_file, temp_dir = extract_kml_from_kmz(file_path)
            try:
                if self.main_logic.load_kmz(file_path):
                    area = self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres
                    self.polygon_coords = [(pt['lon'], pt['lat']) for pt in self.main_logic.polygon_coords]
                    self.crs_display.setText(self.main_logic.utm_crs)
                    logging.debug(f"Set self.polygon_coords: sample={self.polygon_coords[:2] if self.polygon_coords else None}")
                    self.logger.info(f"Loaded KMZ: {file_path}, Area: {area:.2f} acres, CRS: {self.main_logic.utm_crs}")
                    self.modulus_input.setText(str(self.main_logic.calculate_modulus(area, 26)))
                    if self.dem_check.isChecked():
                        self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DEM...")
                        try:
                            dem_path = self.main_logic.download_dem(file_path)
                            if dem_path:
                                self.dem_input.setText(dem_path)
                                self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DEM: {dem_path}")
                            else:
                                self.logger.error("DEM download failed or returned no path")
                                self.dem_check.setChecked(False)
                                self.dem_input.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dem_button.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dem_input.clear()
                                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", "DEM auto-download failed. Please select a DEM file manually.")
                        except Exception as e:
                            self.logger.error(f"DEM auto-download failed: {e}")
                            self.dem_check.setChecked(False)
                            self.dem_input.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dem_button.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dem_input.clear()
                            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", f"DEM auto-download failed: {e}")
                    if self.dsm_check.isChecked():
                        self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DSM...")
                        try:
                            dsm_path = self.main_logic.download_dsm(file_path)
                            if dsm_path:
                                self.dsm_input.setText(dsm_path)
                                self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DSM: {dsm_path}")
                            else:
                                self.logger.error("DSM download failed or returned no path")
                                self.dsm_check.setChecked(False)
                                self.dsm_input.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dsm_button.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dsm_input.clear()
                                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", "DSM auto-download failed. Please select a DSM file manually.")
                        except Exception as e:
                            self.logger.error(f"DSM auto-download failed: {e}")
                            self.dsm_check.setChecked(False)
                            self.dsm_input.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dsm_button.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dsm_input.clear()
                            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", f"DSM auto-download failed: {e}")
                    self.kmz_loaded = True
                else:
                    self.logger.error("Failed to load KMZ file")
                    QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", "Failed to load KMZ/KML file. Please check the file and try again.")
            finally:
                if temp_dir and os.path.exists(temp_dir):
                    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(temp_dir, topdown=False):
                        for name in files:
                            os.remove(os.path.join(root, name))
                        for name in dirs:
                            os.rmdir(os.path.join(root, name))
                    os.rmdir(temp_dir)
                    logging.debug(f"Cleaned up temporary directory: {temp_dir}")

    def browse_dem(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DEM File", "", "DEM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dem_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DEM: {file_path}")

    def browse_dsm(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DSM File", "", "DSM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dsm_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DSM: {file_path}")

    def set_custom_crs(self):
        custom_crs, ok = QInputDialog.getText(self, "Custom CRS", "Enter EPSG code (e.g., 32617):")
        if ok and custom_crs.isdigit():
            self.crs_display.setText(f"EPSG:{custom_crs}")
            self.main_logic.utm_crs = f"EPSG:{custom_crs}"
            self.logger.info(f"Set custom CRS: EPSG:{custom_crs}")
        else:
            self.crs_display.setText(self.main_logic.utm_crs)
            self.logger.debug("Custom CRS input cancelled or invalid")

    def update_sequence(self):
        sequence_type = self.sequence_combo.currentText()
        modulus = self.modulus_input.text()
        modulus = int(modulus) if modulus.isdigit() else None
        self.main_logic.set_sequence_type(sequence_type, modulus)
        self.logger.debug(f"Updated sequence type to {sequence_type} with modulus {modulus}")

    def generate_plan(self):
        self.logger.debug("Starting plan generation")
        try:
            if not self.kmz_loaded:
                self.logger.error("Cannot generate plan: No KMZ loaded")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Warning", "Please load a KMZ/KML file first.")
                return

            spacing = float(self.spacing_combo.currentText())
            layout_mode = self.layout_combo.currentText()
            dem_path = self.dem_input.text() if self.dem_input.text() and os.path.exists(self.dem_input.text()) else None
            dsm_path = self.dsm_input.text() if self.dsm_input.text() and os.path.exists(self.dsm_input.text()) else None
            accuracy = float(self.accuracy_input.text()) if self.accuracy_input.text() else 6.0
            altitude = float(self.altitude_input.text()) if self.altitude_input.text() else 80.0
            fov = float(self.fov_input.text()) if self.fov_input.text() else 90.0
            prr = 640000
            min_distance_factor = float(self.min_distance_input.text()) if self.min_distance_input.text() else 0.25

            self.logger.debug(f"Generating GCP plan with spacing={spacing}m, layout={layout_mode}")
            result = self.main_logic.generate_gcp_plan(
                spacing, layout_mode, dem_path, dsm_path, min_distance_factor
            )
            self.gcp_points = result['gcp_points']
            self.verification_points = result['verification_points']
            self.rejected_gcp_points = result['rejected_gcp_points']
            self.rejected_verification_points = result['rejected_verification_points']
            self.elevation_data = result.get('elevation_data', {})
            self.diagnostic_report = generate_overlay_diagnostics(self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, layout_mode)
            self.logger.info(f"Generated {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(self.verification_points)} VCPs, "
                           f"{len(self.rejected_gcp_points)} rejected GCPs, {len(self.rejected_verification_points)} rejected VCPs")
            self.logger.info(f"Elevation Profile: min={self.elevation_data.get('min', 0.0):.2f}m, "
                           f"max={self.elevation_data.get('max', 0.0):.2f}m, mean={self.elevation_data.get('mean', 0.0):.2f}m")
            self.logger.info(f"Overlay Diagnostics: {self.diagnostic_report}")

            self.flight_params = self.main_logic.compute_flight_parameters(prr, fov, accuracy, spacing, self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres, altitude)
            self.logger.info(f"Flight Parameters: Accuracy={self.flight_params.get('accuracy_mm', 0.0)}mm, "
                           f"Altitude={self.flight_params.get('altitude_m', 0.0)}m, "
                           f"FOV={self.flight_params.get('fov_deg', 0.0)}deg, "
                           f"PRR={self.flight_params.get('pulse_rate_pps', 0)/1000}kHz, "
                           f"Speed={self.flight_params.get('speed_mps', 0.0)}m/s, "
                           f"Resolution={self.flight_params.get('gsd_mm', 0.0)/10:.2f}cm/pixel")
            self.review_button.setEnabled(True)
            self.export_button.setEnabled(True)
            self.kmz_loaded = True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Plan generation failed: {str(e)}")
            QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", f"Plan generation failed: {str(e)}")

    def review_points(self):
        try:

                self.export_button.setEnabled(True)
            else:

        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to open point editor: {e}")
            QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", f"Failed to open point editor: {e}")

UTM Zone Auto-Detection
The get_utm_zone function from utils.py auto-detects UTM zones based on the centroid longitude of the survey area’s coordinates:

Uses shapely.geometry.Polygon to compute the centroid.
Calculates the zone: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Returns EPSG code (e.g., EPSG:32617 for Zone 17N, assuming Northern Hemisphere based on log latitudes ~39°N).

utils.py (Reference)
Purpose: Shared utilities, including UTM zone auto-detection.
Code:

python
import logging
from shapely.geometry import Polygon
import math

# Configure logging
logging.basicConfig(
    filename="uas_survey_tool.log",
    level=logging.DEBUG,
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"
)

def get_utm_zone(coordinates):
    """
    Auto-detect UTM zone from coordinates.
    
    Args:
        coordinates (list): List of (lon, lat) tuples.
    
    Returns:
        str: EPSG code (e.g., 'EPSG:32617' for UTM Zone 17N).
    """
    try:
        if not coordinates or len(coordinates) < 3:
            raise ValueError("At least 3 coordinates required for UTM zone detection")

        polygon = Polygon(coordinates)
        centroid = polygon.centroid
        lon = centroid.x
        zone = math.floor((lon + 180) / 6) + 1
        hemisphere = "N" if centroid.y >= 0 else "S"
        epsg_code = f"EPSG:{32600 + zone}" if hemisphere == "N" else f"EPSG:{32700 + zone}"
        logging.debug(f"Auto-detected UTM zone: {epsg_code} (lon={lon:.2f}, lat={centroid.y:.2f})")
        return epsg_code
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"UTM zone detection failed: {e}")
        raise

def resource_path(relative_path):
    """Get absolute path to resource, works for dev and PyInstaller."""
    base_path = getattr(sys, '_MEIPASS', os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
    return os.path.join(base_path, relative_path)

class TextEditHandler(logging.Handler):
    """Custom logging handler to output to QTextEdit."""
    def __init__(self, text_edit):
        super().__init__()
        self.text_edit = text_edit

    def emit(self, record):
        msg = self.format(record).encode('utf-8', errors='replace').decode('utf-8')
        self.text_edit.append(msg)
        self.text_edit.ensureCursorVisible()

    def plot_points(self):
        self.ax.clear()
        try:
            if self.polygon_coords:
                x_poly, y_poly = zip(*self.polygon_coords)
                self.ax.plot(x_poly + (x_poly[0],), y_poly + (y_poly[0],), 'k-', label="Polygon")
            else:
                logging.warning("No polygon coordinates to plot")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Failed to plot polygon: {e}")

        gcp_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        gcp_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        ver_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['ver']]

        rej_gcp_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']]
        rej_gcp_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']]
        rej_ver_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']]
        rej_ver_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']]

        self.gcp_plot = self.ax.scatter(gcp_x, gcp_y, c='blue', marker='o', label="GCPs", alpha=1.0)
        self.ver_plot = self.ax.scatter(ver_x, ver_y, c='red', marker='x', label="Verification Points", alpha=1.0)
        self.rej_gcp_plot = self.ax.scatter(rej_gcp_x, rej_gcp_y, c='red', marker='o', label="Rejected GCPs", alpha=0.3)
        self.rej_ver_plot = self.ax.scatter(rej_ver_x, rej_ver_y, c='orange', marker='x', label="Rejected Verification Points", alpha=0.3)

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['gcp']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['elevation']:.2f}m)", fontsize=8, ha='right', va='bottom')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['ver']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['elevation']:.2f}m)", fontsize=8, ha='left', va='bottom')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['reason']})", fontsize=8, ha='right', va='bottom', color='gray')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], f"{pt['name']} ({pt['reason']})", fontsize=8, ha='left', va='bottom', color='gray')

        self.ax.legend(loc='upper right', bbox_to_anchor=(1.15, 1))
        self.ax.set_xlabel("Easting (m)")
        self.ax.set_ylabel("Northing (m)")
        self.ax.set_aspect('equal')
        self.canvas.draw()

    def on_click(self, event):
        if event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        min_dist = float('inf')
        closest_idx = None
        closest_type = None

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'gcp'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'ver'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'rejected_gcp'
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'rejected_ver'

        if closest_idx is not None:
            if event.button == 1 and not event.dblclick:
                if closest_type in ['gcp', 'ver']:
                    self.dragging = True
                    self.drag_index = closest_idx
                    self.drag_type = closest_type
            elif event.button == 3:
                if closest_type in ['gcp', 'ver', 'rejected_gcp', 'rejected_ver']:
                    item = (
                        self.gcp_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'gcp' else
                        self.ver_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'ver' else
                        self.rejected_gcp_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'rejected_gcp' else
                        self.rejected_ver_list.item(closest_idx)
                    )
                    item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Unchecked if item.checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked else Qt.CheckState.Checked)
                    self.update_selection()
            elif event.button == 1 and event.dblclick and closest_type in ['rejected_gcp', 'rejected_ver']:
                point = self.rejected_gcp_points[closest_idx] if closest_type == 'rejected_gcp' else self.rejected_verification_points[closest_idx]
                if QMessageBox.question(self, "Reintroduce Point", f"Reintroduce {point['name']} ({point['reason']})?") == QMessageBox.StandardButton.Yes:
                    self.reintroduce_point(closest_idx, closest_type)

    def on_double_click(self, event):
        if event.inaxes != self.ax or event.button != 1 or not event.dblclick:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        logging.debug(f"Double-click detected at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        polygon = Polygon(self.polygon_coords)
        if not polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
            logging.warning(f"New point at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}) is outside polygon")
            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Invalid Location", "New point must be within the polygon boundary.")
            return

        point_type, ok = QInputDialog.getItem(self, "Add Point", "Select point type:", ["GCP", "Verification Point"], 0, False)
        if not ok:
            logging.debug("User cancelled point type selection")
            return

        transformer = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        lon, lat = transformer.transform(x, y)
        elevation = 0.0
        if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
            try:
                dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer)
                dem_dataset.close()
                if dsm_dataset:
                    dsm_dataset.close()
                if not suitable:
                    logging.warning(f"New point at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}) rejected: {reason}")
                    QMessageBox.warning(self, "Invalid Location", f"Cannot add point: {reason}")
                    return
                elevation = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Failed to sample elevation for new point: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", f"Failed to sample elevation: {e}")
                return

        if point_type == "GCP":
            name = f"GCP_new_{self.gcp_counter}"
            self.gcp_points.append({
                'lat': lat, 'lon': lon, 'name': name, 'elevation': elevation,
                'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': 0.0, 'global_offset': 0.0,
                'status': 'accepted', 'reason': '', 'type': 'GCP'
            })
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{name} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {elevation:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].add(len(self.gcp_points) - 1)
            self.gcp_counter += 1
            logging.info(f"Added new GCP: {name} at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        else:
            name = f"Veri_new_{self.ver_counter}"
            self.verification_points.append({
                'lat': lat, 'lon': lon, 'name': name, 'elevation': elevation,
                'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': 0.0, 'global_offset': 0.0,
                'status': 'accepted', 'reason': '', 'type': 'VCP'
            })
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{name} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {elevation:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['ver'].add(len(self.verification_points) - 1)
            self.ver_counter += 1
            logging.info(f"Added new Verification Point: {name} at ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        self.plot_points()

    def reintroduce_point(self, index, point_type):
        if point_type == 'rejected_gcp':
            point = self.rejected_gcp_points.pop(index)
            point['status'] = 'accepted'
            point['manually_restored'] = True
            point['original_reason'] = point.get('reason', 'Unknown')
            point['reason'] = ''
            self.gcp_points.append(point)
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{point['name']} ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {point['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].add(len(self.gcp_points) - 1)
            self.reintroduction_history.append(('gcp', index, point))
            logging.info(f"Reintroduced GCP: {point['name']} at ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f})")
        else:
            point = self.rejected_verification_points.pop(index)
            point['status'] = 'accepted'
            point['manually_restored'] = True
            point['original_reason'] = point.get('reason', 'Unknown')
            point['reason'] = ''
            self.verification_points.append(point)
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{point['name']} ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {point['elevation']:.2f}m)")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
            self.selected_points['ver'].add(len(self.verification_points) - 1)
            self.reintroduction_history.append(('ver', index, point))
            logging.info(f"Reintroduced Verification Point: {point['name']} at ({point['easting']:.2f}, {point['northing']:.2f})")
        self.rejected_gcp_list.clear()
        self.rejected_ver_list.clear()
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_ver_list.addItem(item)
        self.undo_button.setEnabled(True)
        self.plot_points()

    def reintroduce_selected(self):
        selected_gcp = [i for i in range(self.rejected_gcp_list.count()) if self.rejected_gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked]
        selected_ver = [i for i in range(self.rejected_ver_list.count()) if self.rejected_ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked]
        for i in reversed(selected_gcp):
            self.reintroduce_point(i, 'rejected_gcp')
        for i in reversed(selected_ver):
            self.reintroduce_point(i, 'rejected_ver')
        self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'].clear()
        self.selected_points['rejected_ver'].clear()

    def undo_reintroduction(self):
        if not self.reintroduction_history:
            return
        point_type, index, point = self.reintroduction_history.pop()
        if point_type == 'gcp':
            self.gcp_points.remove(point)
            point['status'] = 'rejected'
            point['manually_restored'] = False
            point['reason'] = point['original_reason']
            self.rejected_gcp_points.append(point)
            self.gcp_list.takeItem(self.gcp_list.count() - 1)
            self.selected_points['gcp'].discard(len(self.gcp_points))
        else:
            self.verification_points.remove(point)
            point['status'] = 'rejected'
            point['manually_restored'] = False
            point['reason'] = point['original_reason']
            self.rejected_verification_points.append(point)
            self.ver_list.takeItem(self.ver_list.count() - 1)
            self.selected_points['ver'].discard(len(self.verification_points))
        self.rejected_gcp_list.clear()
        self.rejected_ver_list.clear()
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.rejected_verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}, Elev: {pt['elevation']:.2f}m) - {pt['reason']}")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked if i in self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] else Qt.CheckState.Unchecked)
            self.rejected_ver_list.addItem(item)
        self.undo_button.setEnabled(bool(self.reintroduction_history))
        logging.info(f"Undid reintroduction of {point['name']}")
        self.plot_points()

    def on_motion(self, event):
        if not self.dragging or event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        polygon = Polygon(self.polygon_coords)
        if not polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
            return
        transformer = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        if self.drag_type == 'gcp':
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = transformer.transform(x, y)
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            elevation = 0.0
            if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
                try:
                    dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                    dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                    suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer)
                    dem_dataset.close()
                    if dsm_dataset:
                        dsm_dataset.close()
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['elevation'] = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['status'] = 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected'
                    self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['reason'] = reason
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Failed to update elevation for dragged point: {e}")
            self.gcp_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['elevation']:.2f}m)")
        elif self.drag_type == 'ver':
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = transformer.transform(x, y)
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            elevation = 0.0
            if self.dem_path and os.path.exists(self.dem_path):
                try:
                    dem_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dem_path)
                    dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(self.dsm_path) if self.dsm_path and os.path.exists(self.dsm_path) else None
                    suitable, reason, elevation_value = self.main_logic.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer)
                    dem_dataset.close()
                    if dsm_dataset:
                        dsm_dataset.close()
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['elevation'] = float(elevation_value) if elevation_value is not None else 0.0
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['status'] = 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected'
                    self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['reason'] = reason
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.error(f"Failed to update elevation for dragged point: {e}")
            self.ver_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}, Elev: {self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['elevation']:.2f}m)")
        self.plot_points()

    def on_release(self, event):
        self.dragging = False
        self.drag_index = None
        self.drag_type = None

    def update_selection(self):
        self.selected_points['gcp'] = {i for i in range(self.gcp_list.count()) if self.gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['ver'] = {i for i in range(self.ver_list.count()) if self.ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['rejected_gcp'] = {i for i in range(self.rejected_gcp_list.count()) if self.rejected_gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['rejected_ver'] = {i for i in range(self.rejected_ver_list.count()) if self.rejected_ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.plot_points()

    def get_selected_points(self):
        selected_gcp = [self.gcp_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        selected_ver = [self.verification_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        return selected_gcp, selected_ver

class UASWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("UAS Survey Tool v2.0")
        icon_path = resource_path("app_icon.ico")
        self.setWindowIcon(QIcon(icon_path))
        self.main_logic = MainLogic()
        self.gcp_points = []
        self.verification_points = []
        self.rejected_gcp_points = []
        self.rejected_verification_points = []
        self.flight_params = {}
        self.area_name = ""
        self.polygon_coords = []
        self.elevation_data = {}
        self.diagnostic_report = ""
        self.kmz_loaded = False
        self.last_kmz_load_time = 0
        self.debounce_interval = 1.0
        self.init_ui()
        self.setup_logging()
        logging.debug("UASWindow instance created")
        result = self.main_logic.run_core_analysis()
        logging.debug(f"Core analysis result: {result}")

    def setup_logging(self):
        logging.getLogger().handlers = []
        logging.getLogger(__name__).handlers = []
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s", encoding='utf-8')
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        self.logger.propagate = False
        console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        console_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        console_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(console_handler)
        log_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'logs')
        os.makedirs(log_dir, exist_ok=True)
        log_path = os.path.join(log_dir, "uas_survey_tool.log")
        file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_path, encoding='utf-8')
        file_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        file_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(file_handler)
        handler = TextEditHandler(self.status_log)
        handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(handler)
        self.logger.debug(f"Logger handlers after setup: {len(self.logger.handlers)}")

    def init_ui(self):
        screen = QApplication.primaryScreen()
        screen_size = screen.availableGeometry()
        screen_width = screen_size.width()
        screen_height = screen_size.height()
        min_width = max(800, int(screen_width * 0.7))
        min_height = max(600, int(screen_height * 0.7))
        max_width = min(1400, int(screen_width * 0.9))
        max_height = min(1000, int(screen_height * 0.9))
        self.setMinimumSize(min_width, min_height)
        self.setMaximumSize(max_width, max_height)
        self.resize(min_width, 800)
        logging.debug(f"Screen size: {screen_width}x{screen_height}, Min size: {min_width}x{min_height}, Max size: {max_width}x{max_height}")

        scroll_area = QScrollArea()
        scroll_area.setWidgetResizable(True)
        self.setCentralWidget(scroll_area)

        main_widget = QWidget()
        scroll_area.setWidget(main_widget)
        main_layout = QVBoxLayout(main_widget)
        main_layout.setContentsMargins(15, 15, 15, 15)
        main_layout.setSpacing(20)

        font = QFont("Helvetica", 12)
        self.setFont(font)

        input_group = QGroupBox("Input Parameters")
        input_layout = QFormLayout()
        input_layout.setSpacing(10)
        input_layout.setLabelAlignment(Qt.AlignmentFlag.AlignRight)
        input_layout.setContentsMargins(15, 20, 15, 15)

        self.kmz_label = QLabel("KMZ/KML File:")
        self.kmz_label.setToolTip("Select a KMZ/KML file defining the Area of Interest (AOI).")
        kmz_widget = QHBoxLayout()
        self.kmz_input = QLineEdit()
        self.kmz_input.setReadOnly(True)
        self.kmz_input.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.kmz_input.setMinimumHeight(30)
        self.kmz_button = QPushButton("Browse")
        self.kmz_button.setToolTip("Browse for a KMZ/KML file.")
        self.kmz_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.kmz_button.setMinimumWidth(80)
        self.kmz_button.setMinimumHeight(30)
        self.kmz_button.clicked.connect(self.browse_kmz)
        kmz_widget.addWidget(self.kmz_input)
        kmz_widget.addWidget(self.kmz_button)
        input_layout.addRow(self.kmz_label, kmz_widget)

        self.crs_label = QLabel("CRS (Auto-Detected):")
        self.crs_label.setToolTip("CRS is auto-detected from KMZ/KML geolocation; use Custom for manual input.")
        crs_widget = QHBoxLayout()
        self.crs_display = QLabel("Auto-Detecting...")
        self.crs_display.setToolTip("Displays auto-detected CRS or custom input.")
        self.crs_display.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.crs_display.setMinimumHeight(30)
        self.crs_custom_button = QPushButton("Custom")
        self.crs_custom_button.setToolTip("Enter custom EPSG code if needed.")
        self.crs_custom_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.crs_custom_button.setMinimumWidth(80)
        self.crs_custom_button.setMinimumHeight(30)
        self.crs_custom_button.clicked.connect(self.set_custom_crs)
        crs_widget.addWidget(self.crs_display)
        crs_widget.addWidget(self.crs_custom_button)
        input_layout.addRow(self.crs_label, crs_widget)

        self.dem_check = QCheckBox("Auto-Download DEM")
        self.dem_check.setChecked(True)
        self.dem_check.setToolTip("Enable auto-download of a DEM for the KMZ area.")
        self.dem_check.stateChanged.connect(self.toggle_dem_selection)
        input_layout.addRow(self.dem_check)

        self.dem_label = QLabel("DEM File:")
        self.dem_label.setToolTip("Manually select a DEM file if auto-download is disabled.")
        dem_widget = QHBoxLayout()
        self.dem_input = QLineEdit()
        self.dem_input.setReadOnly(True)
        self.dem_input.setEnabled(False)

        self.spacing_combo.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)

        self.min_distance_input = QLineEdit("0.25")
        self.min_distance_input.setToolTip("Set min distance factor (0.1-0.5).")
        self.min_distance_input.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)

        self.layout_label = QLabel("Layout Mode:")

        layout_patterns = [
            ("grid", "Places GCPs in a uniform grid."),
            ("triangular", "Arranges GCPs in a triangular lattice."),
            ("diamond", "Uses a rotated grid for balanced distribution."),
            ("organic", "Randomly places GCPs with controlled spacing."),
            ("spiral", "Distributes GCPs in a spiral pattern."),
            ("golden_ratio", "Uses a golden ratio spiral for natural distribution."),
            ("fibonacci", "Applies Fibonacci sequence for placement."),
            ("chaotic", "Places GCPs in a pseudo-random chaotic pattern."),
            ("fractal", "Applies recursive Fibonacci placement.")
        ]
        for pattern, tooltip in layout_patterns:
            self.layout_combo.addItem(pattern)
            self.layout_combo.setItemData(self.layout_combo.count()-1, tooltip, Qt.ItemDataRole.ToolTipRole)
        self.layout_combo.setCurrentText("grid")
        self.layout_combo.setToolTip("Select layout pattern.")
        self.layout_combo.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.layout_combo.setMinimumHeight(30)

        self.sequence_label = QLabel("Sequence Type:")

        self.sequence_combo = QComboBox()
        sequence_types = [
            ("fibonacci", "Uses Fibonacci sequence for balanced distribution."),
            ("lucas", "Applies Lucas sequence for varied spacing."),
            ("tribonacci", "Employs Tribonacci sequence for denser patterns."),
            ("pell", "Uses Pell sequence for robust distribution.")
        ]
        for seq_type, tooltip in sequence_types:
            self.sequence_combo.addItem(seq_type)
            self.sequence_combo.setItemData(self.sequence_combo.count()-1, tooltip, Qt.ItemDataRole.ToolTipRole)
        self.sequence_combo.setCurrentText("fibonacci")
        self.sequence_combo.setToolTip("Choose sequence type.")
        self.sequence_combo.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.sequence_combo.setMinimumHeight(30)
        self.sequence_combo.currentTextChanged.connect(self.update_sequence)
        input_layout.addRow(self.sequence_label, self.sequence_combo)

        self.modulus_label = QLabel("Modulus:")

        self.modulus_input.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)

        input_group.setLayout(input_layout)
        main_layout.addWidget(input_group)

        flight_group = QGroupBox("Flight Parameters")

        self.altitude_label = QLabel("Flight Altitude (m):")

        self.fov_input.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.fov_input.setMinimumHeight(30)
        flight_layout.addRow(self.fov_label, self.fov_input)

        self.prr_label = QLabel("Pulse Repetition Rate (kHz):")
        self.prr_label.setToolTip("Pulse rate for RECON-XT LiDAR.")
        self.prr_static = QLabel("640")
        self.prr_static.setToolTip("Fixed PRR at 640 kHz.")
        self.prr_static.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.prr_static.setMinimumHeight(30)
        flight_layout.addRow(self.prr_label, self.prr_static)

        button_row = QHBoxLayout()
        self.generate_button = QPushButton("Generate Plan")
        self.generate_button.setObjectName("actionButton")

        self.generate_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.generate_button.setMinimumWidth(120)
