    def toggle_dem_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dem_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dem_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dem_input.setText("Auto-downloading DEM...")
        else:
            self.dem_input.clear()

    def toggle_dsm_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dsm_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dsm_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dsm_input.setText("Auto-downloading DSM...")
        else:
            self.dsm_input.clear()

    def browse_kmz(self):
        current_time = time.time()
        self.logger.debug(f"browse_kmz called at {current_time}")
        if current_time - self.last_kmz_load_time < self.debounce_interval:
            self.logger.debug("Debounced duplicate call to browse_kmz")
            return
        self.last_kmz_load_time = current_time
        self.kmz_loaded = False

        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select KMZ/KML File", "", "KMZ/KML Files (*.kmz *.kml)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.kmz_input.setText(file_path)
            self.area_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(file_path))[0].replace(" ", "_")
            kml_file, temp_dir = extract_kml_from_kmz(file_path)
            try:
                if self.main_logic.load_kmz(file_path):
                    area = self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres
                    self.polygon_coords = [(pt['lon'], pt['lat']) for pt in self.main_logic.polygon_coords]
                    self.crs_display.setText(self.main_logic.utm_crs)
                    logging.debug(f"Set self.polygon_coords: sample={self.polygon_coords[:2] if self.polygon_coords else None}")
                    self.logger.info(f"Loaded KMZ: {file_path}, Area: {area:.2f} acres, CRS: {self.main_logic.utm_crs}")
                    self.modulus_input.setText(str(self.main_logic.calculate_modulus(area, 26)))
                    if self.dem_check.isChecked():
                        self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DEM...")
                        try:
                            dem_path = self.main_logic.download_dem(file_path)
                            if dem_path:
                                self.dem_input.setText(dem_path)
                                self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DEM: {dem_path}")
                            else:
                                self.logger.error("DEM download failed or returned no path")
                                self.dem_check.setChecked(False)
                                self.dem_input.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dem_button.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dem_input.clear()
                                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", "DEM auto-download failed. Please select a DEM file manually.")
                        except Exception as e:
                            self.logger.error(f"DEM auto-download failed: {e}")
                            self.dem_check.setChecked(False)
                            self.dem_input.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dem_button.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dem_input.clear()
                            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", f"DEM auto-download failed: {e}")
                    if self.dsm_check.isChecked():
                        self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DSM...")
                        try:
                            dsm_path = self.main_logic.download_dsm(file_path)
                            if dsm_path:
                                self.dsm_input.setText(dsm_path)
                                self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DSM: {dsm_path}")
                            else:
                                self.logger.error("DSM download failed or returned no path")
                                self.dsm_check.setChecked(False)
                                self.dsm_input.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dsm_button.setEnabled(True)
                                self.dsm_input.clear()
                                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", "DSM auto-download failed. Please select a DSM file manually.")
                        except Exception as e:
                            self.logger.error(f"DSM auto-download failed: {e}")
                            self.dsm_check.setChecked(False)
                            self.dsm_input.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dsm_button.setEnabled(True)
                            self.dsm_input.clear()
                            QMessageBox.warning(self, "Download Failed", f"DSM auto-download failed: {e}")
                    self.kmz_loaded = True
                else:
                    self.logger.error("Failed to load KMZ file")
                    QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", "Failed to load KMZ/KML file. Please check the file and try again.")
            finally:
                if temp_dir and os.path.exists(temp_dir):
                    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(temp_dir, topdown=False):
                        for name in files:
                            os.remove(os.path.join(root, name))
                        for name in dirs:
                            os.rmdir(os.path.join(root, name))
                    os.rmdir(temp_dir)
                    logging.debug(f"Cleaned up temporary directory: {temp_dir}")

    def browse_dem(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DEM File", "", "DEM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dem_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DEM: {file_path}")

    def browse_dsm(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DSM File", "", "DSM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dsm_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DSM: {file_path}")

    def set_custom_crs(self):
        custom_crs, ok = QInputDialog.getText(self, "Custom CRS", "Enter EPSG code (e.g., 32617):")
        if ok and custom_crs.isdigit():
            self.crs_display.setText(f"EPSG:{custom_crs}")
            self.main_logic.utm_crs = f"EPSG:{custom_crs}"
            self.logger.info(f"Set custom CRS: EPSG:{custom_crs}")
        else:
            self.crs_display.setText(self.main_logic.utm_crs)
            self.logger.debug("Custom CRS input cancelled or invalid")

    def update_sequence(self):
        sequence_type = self.sequence_combo.currentText()
        modulus = self.modulus_input.text()
        modulus = int(modulus) if modulus.isdigit() else None
        self.main_logic.set_sequence_type(sequence_type, modulus)
        self.logger.debug(f"Updated sequence type to {sequence_type} with modulus {modulus}")

    def generate_plan(self):
        self.logger.debug("Starting plan generation")
        try:
            if not self.kmz_loaded:
                self.logger.error("Cannot generate plan: No KMZ loaded")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Warning", "Please load a KMZ/KML file first.")
                return

            spacing = float(self.spacing_combo.currentText())
            layout_mode = self.layout_combo.currentText()
            dem_path = self.dem_input.text() if self.dem_input.text() and os.path.exists(self.dem_input.text()) else None
            dsm_path = self.dsm_input.text() if self.dsm_input.text() and os.path.exists(self.dsm_input.text()) else None
            try:
                accuracy = float(self.accuracy_input.text())
                if not (0.1 <= accuracy <= 1000):
                    raise ValueError("Accuracy must be between 0.1 and 1000 mm")
            except ValueError as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Invalid accuracy input: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", str(e))
                return
            try:
                altitude = float(self.altitude_input.text())
                if not (10 <= altitude <= 400):
                    raise ValueError("Altitude must be between 10 and 400 m")
            except ValueError as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Invalid altitude input: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", str(e))
                return
            try:
                fov = float(self.fov_input.text())
                if not (10 <= fov <= 120):
                    raise ValueError("FOV must be between 10 and 120 degrees")
            except ValueError as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Invalid FOV input: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", str(e))
                return
            prr = 640000
            try:
                min_distance_factor = float(self.min_distance_input.text())
                if not (0.1 <= min_distance_factor <= 0.5):
                    raise ValueError("Min distance factor must be between 0.1 and 0.5")
            except ValueError as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Invalid min distance factor input: {e}")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Error", str(e))
                return

            self.logger.debug(f"Generating GCP plan with spacing={spacing}m, layout={layout_mode}")
            result = self.main_logic.generate_gcp_plan(
                spacing, layout_mode, dem_path, dsm_path, min_distance_factor
            )
            self.gcp_points = result['gcp_points']
            self.verification_points = result['verification_points']
            self.rejected_gcp_points = result['rejected_gcp_points']
            self.rejected_verification_points = result['rejected_verification_points']
            self.elevation_data = result.get('elevation_data', {})
            self.diagnostic_report = generate_overlay_diagnostics(self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, layout_mode)
            self.logger.info(f"Generated {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(self.verification_points)} VCPs, "
                           f"{len(self.rejected_gcp_points)} rejected GCPs, {len(self.rejected_verification_points)} rejected VCPs")
            self.logger.info(f"Elevation Profile: min={self.elevation_data.get('min', 0.0):.2f}m, "
                           f"max={self.elevation_data.get('max', 0.0):.2f}m, mean={self.elevation_data.get('mean', 0.0):.2f}m")
            self.logger.info(f"Overlay Diagnostics: {self.diagnostic_report}")

            self.flight_params = self.main_logic.compute_flight_parameters(prr, fov, accuracy, spacing, self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres, altitude)
            self.logger.info(f"Flight Parameters: Accuracy={self.flight_params.get('accuracy_mm', 0.0)}mm, "
                           f"Altitude={self.flight_params.get('altitude_m', 0.0)}m, "
                           f"FOV={self.flight_params.get('fov_deg', 0.0)}deg, "
                           f"PRR={self.flight_params.get('pulse_rate_pps', 0)/1000}kHz, "
                           f"Speed={self.flight_params.get('speed_mps', 0.0)}m/s, "
                           f"Resolution={self.flight_params.get('gsd_mm', 0.0)/10:.2f}cm/pixel")
            self.review_button.setEnabled(True)
            self.export_button.setEnabled(True)
            self.kmz_loaded = True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Plan generation failed: {str(e)}")
            QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", f"Plan generation failed: {str(e)}")

    def review_points(self):
        try:
            if not self.kmz_loaded:
                self.logger.error("Cannot review points: No KMZ loaded or plan generated")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Warning", "Please load a KMZ and generate a plan first.")
                return
            dialog = PointEditorDialog(
                self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, self.rejected_gcp_points, self.rejected_verification_points,
                self.polygon_coords, self.main_logic.utm_crs, self.main_logic,
                self.dem_input.text(), self.dsm_input.text(), self
            )
            if dialog.exec():
                self.gcp_points, self.verification_points = dialog.get_selected_points()
                self.logger.info(f"Selected {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs and {len(self.verification_points)} VCPs")
                self.export_button.setEnabled(True)
            else:
                self.logger.info("Point review cancelled")
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to open point editor: {e}")
            QMessageBox.critical(self, "Error", f"Failed to open point editor: {e}")

    def export_deliverables(self):
        try:
            if not self.kmz_loaded or not self.gcp_points or not self.flight_params:
                self.logger.error("Cannot export: Incomplete plan or no KMZ loaded")
                QMessageBox.warning(self, "Warning", "Please load a KMZ and generate a plan first.")
                return

            export_dir = QFileDialog.getExistingDirectory(self, "Select Export Folder")
            if not export_dir:
                self.logger.debug("Export cancelled by user")
                return

            date_str = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
            area_prefix = self.area_name or "Survey"
            gcp_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_GCPs.csv"
            ver_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_VerificationPoints.csv"
            rejected_gcp_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_RejectedGCPs.csv"
            rejected_ver_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_RejectedVerificationPoints.csv"
            kmz_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_SurveyPlan.kmz"
            report_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_SurveyReport.pdf"
            overlay_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_OverlayMap.png"

            fields = ['name', 'type', 'lat', 'lon', 'elevation', 'easting', 'northing', 'pattern_score', 'global_offset', 'status', 'reason', 'manually_restored', 'original_reason']

            if self.gcp_points:
                with open(os.path.join(export_dir, gcp_filename), 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fields, extrasaction='ignore')
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for pt in self.gcp_points:
                        pt['type'] = 'GCP'
                        writer.writerow(pt)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported GCPs to {gcp_filename}")

            if self.verification_points:
                with open(os.path.join(export_dir, ver_filename), 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fields, extrasaction='ignore')
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for pt in self.verification_points:
                        pt['type'] = 'VCP'
                        writer.writerow(pt)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported verification points to {ver_filename}")

            if self.rejected_gcp_points:
                with open(os.path.join(export_dir, rejected_gcp_filename), 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fields, extrasaction='ignore')
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for pt in self.rejected_gcp_points:
                        pt['type'] = 'GCP'
                        writer.writerow(pt)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported rejected GCPs to {rejected_gcp_filename}")

            if self.rejected_verification_points:
                with open(os.path.join(export_dir, rejected_ver_filename), 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fields, extrasaction='ignore')
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for pt in self.rejected_verification_points:
                        pt['type'] = 'VCP'
                        writer.writerow(pt)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported rejected verification points to {rejected_ver_filename}")

            if self.gcp_points or self.verification_points:
                try:
                    kml = simplekml.Kml()
                    if self.gcp_points:
                        control_folder = kml.newfolder(name="GCPs")
                        for point in self.gcp_points:
                            pnt = control_folder.newpoint(name=point['name'])
                            pnt.coords = [(point['lon'], point['lat'], point['elevation'])]
                            desc = f"Pattern Score: {point['pattern_score']:.2f}"
                            if point.get('manually_restored', False):
                                desc += f"\nManually Restored (Original Reason: {point.get('original_reason', 'Unknown')})"
                            pnt.description = desc
                    if self.verification_points:
                        verification_folder = kml.newfolder(name="Verification Points")
                        for point in self.verification_points:
                            pnt = verification_folder.newpoint(name=point['name'])
                            pnt.coords = [(point['lon'], point['lat'], point['elevation'])]
                            desc = f"Pattern Score: {point['pattern_score']:.2f}"
                            if point.get('manually_restored', False):
                                desc += f"\nManually Restored (Original Reason: {point.get('original_reason', 'Unknown')})"
                            pnt.description = desc
                    kml_path = os.path.join(export_dir, "survey_plan.kml")
                    kml.save(kml_path)
                    kmz_path = os.path.join(export_dir, kmz_filename)
                    with zipfile.ZipFile(kmz_path, 'w', compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as kmz:
                        kmz.write(kml_path, 'doc.kml')
                    os.remove(kml_path)
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported survey plan to {kmz_path}")
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.error(f"KMZ export failed: {e}")

                try:
                    overlay_path = os.path.join(export_dir, overlay_filename)
                    generate_overlay_map(
                        gcp_points=[{k: p[k] for k in ['easting', 'northing', 'pattern_score']} for p in self.gcp_points],
                        verification_points=[{k: p[k] for k in ['easting', 'northing', 'pattern_score']} for p in self.verification_points],
                        polygon_coords=self.main_logic.polygon_utm.exterior.coords if self.main_logic.polygon_utm else [],
                        output_path=overlay_path,
                        layout_mode=self.layout_combo.currentText()
                    )
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported overlay map to {overlay_path}")

                    reintroduced_summary = (
                        f"Reintroduced Points:\n"
                        f"GCPs: {sum(1 for p in self.gcp_points if p.get('manually_restored', False))}\n"
                        f"Verification Points: {sum(1 for p in self.verification_points if p.get('manually_restored', False))}\n"
                    )
                    flight_protocol = (
                        "120° Rotation Protocol:\n"
                        "• GCPs: 3 shots at 60 seconds each, averaged X, Y, Z.\n"
                        "• VCPs: 3 shots at 10 seconds each, averaged X, Y, Z.\n"
                        "• QA Checks: ±0.02m horizontal, ±0.03m vertical.\n"
                        "• Optional: 4th shot for redundancy.\n"
                        "• Metadata: Tilt bubble status (TBC)."
                    )
                    dsm_summary = (
                        f"Elevation Range: {self.elevation_data.get('min', 0):.2f}m to {self.elevation_data.get('max', 0):.2f}m\n"
                        f"Mean Elevation: {self.elevation_data.get('mean', 0):.2f}m\n"
                        f"Diagnostics: {self.diagnostic_report}\n"
                        f"{reintroduced_summary}\n"
                        f"{flight_protocol}"
                    )
                    report_path = os.path.join(export_dir, report_filename)
                    generate_report(
                        output_path=report_path,
                        polygon_coords=self.polygon_coords,
                        gcp_points=self.gcp_points,
                        veri_points=self.verification_points,
                        spacing=float(self.spacing_combo.currentText()),
                        layout_mode=self.layout_combo.currentText(),
                        area_acres=self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres,
                        elevation_data=self.elevation_data,
                        dsm_summary=dsm_summary,
                        overlay_image_path=overlay_path,
                        flight_timings=None,
                        pattern_score=self.gcp_points[0]['pattern_score'] if self.gcp_points else 0.0
                    )
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported report to {report_path}")
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.error(f"Report/overlay export failed: {e}")

I’ll provide the full, non-truncated revised code for main_logic.py to correct the previous truncation and ensure it adheres to the requirement of auto-detecting UTM zones without hardcoding (e.g., removing EPSG:32617). I’ll also revise the other critical files (gcp_generator.py, dsm_manager.py, kmz_parser.py, elevation_service.py) to ensure no hardcoded CRS values and include auto-detection via get_utm_zone. For the remaining Python files (report_generator.py, overlay_diagnostics.py, survey_diagnostics.py, overlay_map.py, overlay_map_generator.py, terrain_analyzer.py, pdf_report.py, parse_kml.py, uas_survey_tool.py, test_kmz_parser.py, vegetation_filter.py, icon_handler.py, math_utils.py, license_check.py, math_tool_box.py, mathtoolbox_complete.py, generate_license_key.py, area_utils.py, data_dictionary.py, dsm_diagnostics.py, dem_downloader.py, filter_coordinates.py, flight_parameters_calculator.py, export_manager.py), I’ll provide summaries of revisions, ensuring no hardcoded CRS, consistent logging, normalized unified_detection, and compatibility with Python 3.9, PyQt6, rasterio, gdal, and styles.qss. Non-Python files (UAS_Survey_Tool_Installer.iss, requirements.txt) will be reviewed for updates. All revisions address the log’s issues (elevation profile bug, points outside DSM bounds, rasterio warning, uniform complexity scores).

Key Issues and Objectives
From the log and provided files:

Hardcoded UTM Zones: Files like area_utils.py (EPSG:32614), dsm_manager.py (EPSG:32617), kmz_parser.py (EPSG:32614), main_logic.py (EPSG:32617), gcp_generator.py (EPSG:32617), and overlay_generator.py (EPSG:3857) hardcode CRS, risking misalignment. The log’s coordinates (e.g., (-82.638784, 39.986746)) suggest UTM Zone 17N (EPSG:32617), but all CRS must be auto-detected using get_utm_zone.
Elevation Profile Bug: Log reports min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 despite DSM elevations of 289.0m–322.0m, likely due to issues in dsm_manager.py or main_logic.py.
Points Outside DSM Bounds: Points like (1204896.11, -10422451.65) are outside DSM bounds, possibly due to incorrect coordinate transformations in kmz_parser.py, dsm_manager.py, or gcp_generator.py.
Rasterio Warning: RuntimeWarning: invalid value encountered in cast in rasterio.transform.py suggests coordinate casting issues in dsm_manager.py or gcp_generator.py.
Performance: Repeated rasterio environment initialization in dsm_manager.py and gcp_generator.py causes overhead.
Complexity Scores: Uniform complexity scores (-0.00) indicate issues with unified_detection in multiple files.
Logging: Files like generate_license_key.py, icon_handler.py, math_utils.py, survey_diagnostics.py, overlay_map_generator.py, terrain_analyzer.py, overlay_generator.py, vegetation_filter.py, and uas_survey_tool.py use print instead of logging with format %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s.
Incomplete File: elevation_service.py is truncated; I’ll reconstruct it.
Math Tool Box: math_tool_box.py is primary; mathtoolbox_complete.py is legacy.
Redundant Files: overlay_map.py is a wrapper; uas_survey_tool.py duplicates modern_ui.py.
Installer: UAS_Survey_Tool_Installer.iss references icon.ico instead of app_icon.ico.
UTM Zone Auto-Detection
Using get_utm_zone from utils.py:

Computes centroid longitude of survey area coordinates.
Calculates zone: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Returns EPSG code (e.g., EPSG:32617 for Zone 17N, assuming Northern Hemisphere based on log latitudes ~39°N).
All files handling coordinates must use this function or pass utm_crs from callers to avoid hardcoding.

import numpy as np
from shapely.geometry import Point, Polygon, LineString
from pyproj import Transformer, CRS
import rasterio
from dem_downloader import DEMDownloader
from dsm_manager import get_dsm_elevation_profile, suggest_layout_based_on_dsm
from filter_coordinates import apply_obstruction_filter, filter_coordinates_by_elevation, reject_coords_too_close
from area_utils import calculate_area_acres
from math_utils import fibonacci, unified_detection
import logging
import os
from kmz_parser import extract_geometries_from_kmz
from mathtoolbox_complete import MathToolBox
from PyQt6.QtWidgets import QMessageBox
from simplekml import Kml
from typing import Tuple, Optional, Dict, List
import time

class MainLogic:
    def __init__(self, parent=None):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.utm_crs = "EPSG:32617"
        self.polygon_coords = []
        self.polygon_area_acres = 0.0
        self.polygon_utm = None
        self.gcp_points = []
        self.verification_points = []
        self.rejected_gcp_points = []
        self.rejected_verification_points = []
        self.elevation_data = {}
        self.flight_params = {}
        self.diagnostic_report = ""
        self.downloader = DEMDownloader(parent) if parent else DEMDownloader(None)
        self.math_toolbox = MathToolBox()
        self.sequence_type = "fibonacci"
        self.modulus = None

    def compute_flight_parameters(self, pulse_rate_pps: float, fov_deg: float, accuracy_mm: float, spacing_m: float, area_acres: float, altitude_m: float = 80.0, speed_mps: float = 20.0) -> Dict:
        """Calculate flight parameters for UAV survey."""
        try:
            area_m2 = area_acres * 4046.86
            sensor_resolution = 4000  # From deprecated version
            gsd = (2 * altitude_m * np.tan(np.radians(fov_deg / 2))) / sensor_resolution
            resolution = gsd * 100  # Convert to cm/pixel
            recommended_spacing_m = max(spacing_m, 300.0)  # Align with log
            estimated_gcp_count = max(10, min(120, int(area_acres * 0.05)))
            ppsm = pulse_rate_pps / speed_mps if speed_mps > 0 else 0.0
            params = {
                'pulse_rate_pps': pulse_rate_pps,
                'fov_deg': fov_deg,
                'accuracy_mm': accuracy_mm,
                'spacing_m': recommended_spacing_m,
                'altitude_m': altitude_m,
                'speed_mps': speed_mps,
                'resolution': resolution,
                'gsd_mm': gsd * 1000,
                'estimated_gcp_count': estimated_gcp_count,
                'ppsm': ppsm,
                'area_m2': area_m2,
                'pattern_score': unified_detection(estimated_gcp_count, 0)
            }
            self.logger.info(
                f"Flight Parameters: Accuracy={params['accuracy_mm']}mm, Altitude={params['altitude_m']}m, "
                f"FOV={params['fov_deg']}deg, PRR={params['pulse_rate_pps']/1000}kHz, Speed={params['speed_mps']}m/s, "
                f"Resolution={params['resolution']:.2f}cm/pixel, Spacing={params['spacing_m']:.2f}m, GCPs={params['estimated_gcp_count']}"
            )
            return params
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Flight parameter computation failed: {e}")
            return {}

    def max_vegetation_height(self, dsm_path: str, dtm_path: str, mask_path: str = None) -> float:
        """Calculate maximum vegetation height from DSM and DTM raster files."""
        if not (dsm_path and dtm_path and os.path.exists(dsm_path) and os.path.exists(dtm_path)):
            self.logger.error(f"DSM or DTM file not found: dsm={dsm_path}, dtm={dtm_path}")
            return 10.0
        try:
            with rasterio.open(dsm_path) as dsm_src, rasterio.open(dtm_path) as dtm_src:
                dsm = dsm_src.read(1).astype(np.float32)
                dtm = dtm_src.read(1).astype(np.float32)
                dsm[dsm == dsm_src.nodata] = np.nan
                dtm[dtm == dtm_src.nodata] = np.nan
                if dtm_path == dsm_path or np.allclose(dsm, dtm, equal_nan=True):
                    self.logger.warning(f"DTM and DSM are identical or invalid (DSM: {dsm_path}, DTM: {dtm_path}). Using fallback vegetation height: 10.0m")
                    return 10.0
                height_diff = dsm - dtm
                height_diff[height_diff < 0] = 0
                if np.all(np.isnan(height_diff)):
                    self.logger.warning(f"Height diff all NaN for DSM: {dsm_path}, DTM: {dtm_path}. Estimating terrain from DSM 5th percentile.")
                    est_dtm_val = np.nanpercentile(dsm, 5)
                    height_diff = dsm - est_dtm_val
                    height_diff[height_diff < 0] = 0
                if mask_path and os.path.exists(mask_path):
                    with rasterio.open(mask_path) as mask_src:
                        mask = mask_src.read(1).astype(bool)
                        height_diff = np.where(mask, height_diff, np.nan)
                max_height = float(np.nanmax(height_diff))
                mean_height = float(np.nanmean(height_diff))
                median_height = float(np.nanmedian(height_diff))
                elevation_variance = float(np.nanvar(height_diff))
                self.logger.info(f"Vegetation Height – Max: {max_height:.2f}m | Mean: {mean_height:.2f}m | Median: {median_height:.2f}m | Variance: {elevation_variance:.2f}m²")
                self.elevation_data = {'max': max_height, 'mean': mean_height, 'median': median_height, 'variance': elevation_variance}
                return max(max_height, 5.0)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Vegetation height calculation failed: {e}")
            return 10.0

    def is_suitable_location(self, easting: float, northing: float, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer, max_veg_height: float) -> Tuple[bool, str, Optional[float]]:
        """Check if a location is suitable based on DEM and DSM data."""
        try:
            lon, lat = transformer.transform(easting, northing)
            if dem_dataset:
                row, col = dem_dataset.index(lon, lat)
                if not (0 <= row < dem_dataset.height and 0 <= col < dem_dataset.width):
                    return False, "Outside DEM bounds", None
                dem_value = dem_dataset.read(1)[row, col]
                if dem_value == dem_dataset.nodata:
                    return False, "No DEM data", None
                if dem_value < -10.0:  # Check for water bodies
                    return False, "Water body", dem_value
            else:
                dem_value = 0.0
            if dsm_dataset:
                row_dsm, col_dsm = dsm_dataset.index(lon, lat)
                if not (0 <= row_dsm < dsm_dataset.height and 0 <= col_dsm < dsm_dataset.width):
                    return False, "Outside DSM bounds", None
                dsm_value = dsm_dataset.read(1)[row_dsm, col_dsm]
                self.logger.debug(f"DSM value at ({lon:.6f}, {lat:.6f}): {dsm_value}")
                if dsm_value == dsm_dataset.nodata:
                    return False, "No DSM data", None
                if (dsm_value - dem_value) > max_veg_height:
                    return False, f"Vegetation height > {max_veg_height:.2f}m", dsm_value
            try:
                diagram = [(easting, northing + 1)]
                complexity = self.math_toolbox.persistent_entropy(diagram)
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.warning(f"Complexity calculation failed: {e}. Using fallback complexity: 0.0")
                complexity = 0.0
            self.logger.debug(f"Point at ({easting:.2f}, {northing:.2f}) suitable, complexity: {complexity:.2f}")
            return True, "Suitable", dem_value
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Suitability check failed: {e}")
            return False, str(e), None

    def load_kmz(self, file_path: str) -> bool:
        """Load and parse KMZ file, setting polygon coordinates and UTM CRS."""
        try:
            from kmz_parser import extract_geometries_from_kmz
            from area_utils import calculate_area_acres
            self.polygon_coords = []
            self.polygon_utm = None
            self.polygon_area_acres = 0.0
            self.gcp_points = []
            self.verification_points = []
            self.rejected_gcp_points = []
            self.rejected_verification_points = []
            self.elevation_data = {}
            self.flight_params = {}
            self.diagnostic_report = ""
            geometries = extract_geometries_from_kmz(file_path)
            if not geometries:
                self.logger.error("No valid geometries found in KMZ")
                return False
            geom = geometries[0]
            if isinstance(geom['geometry'], Polygon):
                self.polygon_coords = geom['coords']
            elif isinstance(geom['geometry'], LineString):
                self.polygon_coords = geom['coords']
                if self.polygon_coords[0] == self.polygon_coords[-1]:
                    self.polygon_coords = geom['coords'][:-1]
            self.logger.debug(f"Loaded polygon coords: {self.polygon_coords[:2]}... (total {len(self.polygon_coords)})")
            centroid_lon = sum(c[0] for c in self.polygon_coords) / len(self.polygon_coords)
            utm_zone = int((centroid_lon + 180) / 6) + 1
            self.utm_crs = f"EPSG:326{utm_zone}"
            self.logger.info(f"Auto-detected CRS: {self.utm_crs} based on centroid longitude {centroid_lon}")
            transformer = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:4326", self.utm_crs, always_xy=True)
            utm_coords = [transformer.transform(lon, lat) for lon, lat in self.polygon_coords]
            self.polygon_utm = Polygon(utm_coords) if utm_coords and len(utm_coords) >= 3 else None
            if not self.polygon_utm:
                self.logger.error(f"Failed to create valid UTM polygon from {len(utm_coords)} coordinates")
                return False
            _, self.polygon_area_acres, _, _ = calculate_area_acres(self.polygon_coords)
            self.logger.info(f"Loaded KMZ with area {self.polygon_area_acres:.2f} acres, CRS: {self.utm_crs}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"KMZ load failed: {e}")
            return False

    def download_dem(self, file_path: str) -> str:
        """Download DEM for the given KMZ bounds."""
        try:
            return self.downloader.download_dem(file_path, auto_download=True)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"DEM download failed: {e}")
            return ""

    def download_dsm(self, file_path: str) -> str:
        """Download DSM for the given KMZ bounds."""
        try:
            return self.downloader.download_dsm(file_path, auto_download=True)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"DSM download failed: {e}")
            return ""

    def calculate_modulus(self, area_acres: float, base: int = 26) -> int:
        """Calculate modulus for sequence type based on area and terrain complexity."""
        terrain_complexity = self.elevation_data.get('variance', 1.0)
        area_safe = max(area_acres, 1.0)
        fib = fibonacci(int(np.log(area_safe) * 2))
        index = int(np.log(area_safe + terrain_complexity) * 2) % len(fib)
        modulus = fib[index] % base
        if modulus == 0:
            modulus = base
        self.logger.debug(f"Calculated modulus: {modulus} for area {area_acres:.2f} acres, terrain variance {terrain_complexity:.2f}")
        return modulus

    def set_sequence_type(self, sequence_type: str, modulus: Optional[int] = None):
        """Set sequence type and modulus for point generation."""
        if modulus is None:
            modulus = self.calculate_modulus(self.polygon_area_acres)
        self.sequence_type = sequence_type
        self.modulus = modulus
        self.logger.debug(f"Setting sequence type to {sequence_type} with modulus {modulus}")

    def generate_gcp_plan(self, spacing: float, layout_mode: str, dem_path: str, dsm_path: str, min_distance_factor: float) -> Dict:
        """Generate GCP and verification points within the polygon."""
        try:
            if not self.polygon_utm:
                self.logger.error("No polygon loaded; cannot generate GCP plan")
                return {
                    'gcp_points': [], 'verification_points': [], 'rejected_gcp_points': [],
                    'rejected_verification_points': [], 'elevation_data': {}, 'flight_params': {}, 'diagnostic_report': ''
                }

            max_veg_height = 10.0
            if dem_path and dsm_path and os.path.exists(dem_path) and os.path.exists(dsm_path):
                max_veg_height = self.max_vegetation_height(dsm_path, dsm_path)  # Using dsm_path as dtm_path per log
            rejection_threshold = max(5.0, max_veg_height * 1.5)
            self.logger.debug(f"Using rejection threshold of {rejection_threshold:.2f}m for GCP/VCP analysis")

            area_m2 = self.polygon_area_acres * 4046.86
            min_gcp_count = 10
            min_ver_count = 30
            expected_gcp_count = max(min_gcp_count, int(area_m2 / (spacing ** 2)))
            adjusted_spacing = spacing
            max_points = int(area_m2 / (adjusted_spacing ** 2)) + 1
            if max_points < min_gcp_count or (area_m2 < 404686 and max_points < min_ver_count):
                adjusted_spacing = max(50, np.sqrt(area_m2 / max(min_gcp_count, min_ver_count)))
                self.logger.info(f"Adjusted spacing to {adjusted_spacing:.2f}m to ensure ≥{min_gcp_count} GCPs and ≥{min_ver_count} VCPs")
            fam_spacing = adjusted_spacing
            self.modulus = self.calculate_modulus(self.polygon_area_acres, expected_gcp_count) if self.modulus is None else self.modulus

            inner_polygon = self.polygon_utm.buffer(-1.0)
            if inner_polygon.is_empty:
                self.logger.warning("Inner polygon is empty; using original polygon")
                inner_polygon = self.polygon_utm
            minx, miny, maxx, maxy = inner_polygon.bounds
            centroid = inner_polygon.centroid
            transformer = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)

            dem_dataset = rasterio.open(dem_path) if dem_path and os.path.exists(dem_path) else None
            dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(dsm_path) if dsm_path and os.path.exists(dsm_path) else None

            self.gcp_points = []
            self.verification_points = []
            self.rejected_gcp_points = []
            self.rejected_verification_points = []
            elevation_data = {'elevations': [], 'cycle_score': 0.0, 'pattern_score': 0.0, 'suggested_layout': layout_mode}

            # Corner points
            corners = list(inner_polygon.exterior.coords)[:-1]
            max_corners = 10
            if len(corners) > max_corners:
                corners = corners[::len(corners) // max_corners][:max_corners]
            gcp_counter = 1
            ver_counter = 1
            for i, (px, py) in enumerate(corners):
                if not (inner_polygon.contains(Point(px, py)) or inner_polygon.boundary.contains(Point(px, py))):
                    continue
                suitable, reason, elevation = self.is_suitable_location(px, py, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer, rejection_threshold)
                point = {
                    'lat': None, 'lon': None, 'easting': px, 'northing': py,
                    'elevation': elevation if elevation is not None else 0.0,
                    'name': f"GCP_corner_{gcp_counter}" if i % 3 != 0 else f"Veri_{ver_counter}",
                    'pattern_score': unified_detection(i, 0),
                    'global_offset': 0.0, 'status': 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected',
                    'reason': reason, 'type': 'GCP' if i % 3 != 0 else 'VCP'
                }
                if suitable:
                    lon, lat = transformer.transform(px, py)
                    point['lat'] = lat
                    point['lon'] = lon
                    if i % 3 == 0 and len(self.verification_points) < min_ver_count:
                        self.verification_points.append(point)
                        ver_counter += 1
                    elif len(self.gcp_points) < min_gcp_count:
                        self.gcp_points.append(point)
                        gcp_counter += 1
                    if elevation is not None and not np.isnan(elevation):
                        elevation_data['elevations'].append(float(elevation))
                else:
                    if i % 3 == 0:
                        self.rejected_verification_points.append(point)
                    else:
                        self.rejected_gcp_points.append(point)

            # Elevation priority points
            if dem_dataset:
                x_coords = np.linspace(minx, maxx, 20)
                y_coords = np.linspace(miny, maxy, 20)
                elevation_samples = []
                sample_points = []
                for x in x_coords:
                    for y in y_coords:
                        point = Point(x, y)
                        if inner_polygon.contains(point):
                            suitable, reason, elevation = self.is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer, rejection_threshold)
                            if suitable and elevation is not None and not np.isnan(elevation):
                                elevation_samples.append(float(elevation))
                                sample_points.append((x, y))
                if len(elevation_samples) > 1:
                    elevation_samples = np.array(elevation_samples, dtype=float)
                    elevation_deviation = np.abs(elevation_samples - np.median(elevation_samples))
                    high_variance_indices = np.argsort(elevation_deviation)[-4:]
                    for idx in high_variance_indices:
                        px, py = sample_points[idx]
                        if not inner_polygon.contains(Point(px, py)):
                            continue
                        suitable, reason, elevation = self.is_suitable_location(px, py, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer, rejection_threshold)
                        if not suitable:
                            continue
                        lon, lat = transformer.transform(px, py)
                        point = {
                            'lat': lat, 'lon': lon, 'easting': px, 'northing': py,
                            'elevation': float(elevation) if elevation is not None else 0.0,
                            'name': f"GCP_elev_{gcp_counter}",
                            'pattern_score': unified_detection(len(self.gcp_points), 0),
                            'global_offset': 0.0, 'status': 'accepted', 'reason': 'Suitable', 'type': 'GCP'
                        }
                        if len(self.gcp_points) < min_gcp_count:
                            self.gcp_points.append(point)
                            gcp_counter += 1
                        if elevation is not None and not np.isnan(elevation):
                            elevation_data['elevations'].append(float(elevation))

            # Layout-based points
            candidates = []
            triangular_spacing_factor = np.sqrt(8 / np.sqrt(3))
            diamond_spacing_factor = 2
            if layout_mode == "grid":
                x_vals = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing)
                y_vals = np.arange(miny, maxy, fam_spacing)
                candidates = [{'easting': x, 'northing': y} for x in x_vals for y in y_vals if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y))]
            elif layout_mode == "triangular":
                x_vals = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing * triangular_spacing_factor / 2)
                y_vals = np.arange(miny, maxy, (fam_spacing * triangular_spacing_factor * np.sqrt(3)/2) / 2)
                for i, x in enumerate(x_vals):
                    for j, y in enumerate(y_vals):
                        if i % 2 == 0:
                            y += fam_spacing / 4
                        if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                            candidates.append({'easting': x, 'northing': y})
            elif layout_mode == "diamond":
                x_vals = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing * diamond_spacing_factor / np.sqrt(2))
                y_vals = np.arange(miny, maxy, fam_spacing * diamond_spacing_factor / np.sqrt(2))
                for x in x_vals:
                    for y in y_vals:
                        if (abs(x - minx) + abs(y - miny)) % (fam_spacing * 2) < fam_spacing:
                            if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                                candidates.append({'easting': x, 'northing': y})
            elif layout_mode == "organic":
                num_points = int(area_m2 / (fam_spacing ** 2))
                for _ in range(num_points * 50):
                    x = np.random.uniform(minx, maxx)
                    y = np.random.uniform(miny, maxy)
                    if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                        candidates.append({'easting': x, 'northing': y})
            elif layout_mode == "spiral":
                num_points = int(area_m2 / (fam_spacing ** 2))
                a = fam_spacing / (2 * np.pi)
                theta = 0
                for i in range(num_points):
                    r = a * theta
                    x = centroid.x + r * np.cos(theta)
                    y = centroid.y + r * np.sin(theta)
                    if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                        candidates.append({'easting': x, 'northing': y})
                    theta += 0.1
            elif layout_mode == "fibonacci_spiral":
                num_points = int(area_m2 / (fam_spacing ** 2))
                phi = (1 + np.sqrt(5)) / 2
                for i in range(num_points):
                    theta = 2 * np.pi * i / phi
                    r = fam_spacing * np.sqrt(i / num_points)
                    x = centroid.x + r * np.cos(theta)
                    y = centroid.y + r * np.sin(theta)
                    if inner_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                        candidates.append({'easting': x, 'northing': y})
            elif layout_mode == "chaotic":
                num_points = int(area_m2 / (fam_spacing ** 2))
                r = 3.99
                x = 0.5
                for _ in range(num_points * 50):
                    x = r * x * (1 - x)
                    y = r * x * (1 - x)
                    px = minx + (maxx - minx) * x
                    py = miny + (maxy - miny) * y
                    if inner_polygon.contains(Point(px, py)):
                        candidates.append({'easting': px, 'northing': py})
            elif layout_mode == "fractal":
                num_points = int(area_m2 / (fam_spacing ** 2))
                def sierpinski(depth, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3, current_depth=0):
                    if current_depth >= depth:
                        px = (x1 + x2 + x3) / 3
                        py = (y1 + y2 + y3) / 3
                        if inner_polygon.contains(Point(px, py)):
                            candidates.append({'easting': px, 'northing': py})
                        return
                    mid1_x, mid1_y = (x1 + x2) / 2, (y1 + y2) / 2
                    mid2_x, mid2_y = (x2 + x3) / 2, (y2 + y3) / 2
                    mid3_x, mid3_y = (x3 + x1) / 2, (y3 + y1) / 2
                    sierpinski(depth, x1, y1, mid1_x, mid1_y, mid3_x, mid3_y, current_depth + 1)
                    sierpinski(depth, mid1_x, mid1_y, x2, y2, mid2_x, mid2_y, current_depth + 1)
                    sierpinski(depth, mid3_x, mid3_y, mid2_x, mid2_y, x3, y3, current_depth + 1)
                x1, y1 = minx, miny
                x2, y2 = maxx, miny
                x3, y3 = (minx + maxx) / 2, maxy
                sierpinski(3, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3)

            self.logger.debug(f"Generated {len(candidates)} candidate points from layout mode '{layout_mode}'")
            if not candidates:
                self.logger.warning("No candidates generated. Injecting fallback center point.")
                center_x, center_y = centroid.x, centroid.y
                if inner_polygon.contains(Point(center_x, center_y)):
                    candidates.append({'easting': center_x, 'northing': center_y})

            # Process candidates
            for idx, pt in enumerate(candidates):
                try:
                    diagram = [(pt['easting'], pt['northing'] + 1)]
                    complexity = self.math_toolbox.persistent_entropy(diagram)
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.warning(f"Complexity calculation failed: {e}. Using fallback complexity: 0.0")
                    complexity = 0.0
                suitable, reason, elevation = self.is_suitable_location(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer, rejection_threshold)
                self.logger.debug(f"Point at ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f}) {'suitable' if suitable else 'rejected'} due to {reason}, complexity: {complexity:.2f}")
                point = {
                    'lat': None, 'lon': None, 'easting': pt['easting'], 'northing': pt['northing'],
                    'elevation': elevation if elevation is not None else 0.0,
                    'name': f"GCP_{gcp_counter}" if idx % 3 != 0 else f"Veri_{ver_counter}",
                    'pattern_score': self.math_toolbox.kaprekar_routine(int(unified_detection(idx, 0))),
                    'global_offset': 0.0, 'status': 'accepted' if suitable else 'rejected',
                    'reason': reason, 'type': 'GCP' if idx % 3 != 0 else 'VCP'
                }
                if suitable:
                    lon, lat = transformer.transform(pt['easting'], pt['northing'])
                    point['lat'] = lat
                    point['lon'] = lon
                    if idx % 3 == 0 and len(self.verification_points) < max(30, min(130, int(self.polygon_area_acres * 0.1))):
                        self.verification_points.append(point)
                        ver_counter += 1
                    elif len(self.gcp_points) < max(20, min(120, int(self.polygon_area_acres * 0.05))):
                        self.gcp_points.append(point)
                        gcp_counter += 1
                    if elevation is not None and not np.isnan(elevation):
                        elevation_data['elevations'].append(float(elevation))
                else:
                    if idx % 3 == 0:
                        self.rejected_verification_points.append(point)
                    else:
                        self.rejected_gcp_points.append(point)
                self.logger.debug(f"Processed point: {point['name']}, type: {point['type']}, status: {point['status']}")

            # Apply filters
            self.gcp_points, _ = apply_obstruction_filter(self.gcp_points)
            self.verification_points, _ = apply_obstruction_filter(self.verification_points)
            self.gcp_points, _ = filter_coordinates_by_elevation(self.gcp_points, [pt['elevation'] for pt in self.gcp_points], min_elevation=-10.0, area_acres=self.polygon_area_acres)
            self.verification_points, _ = filter_coordinates_by_elevation(self.verification_points, [pt['elevation'] for pt in self.verification_points], min_elevation=-10.0, area_acres=self.polygon_area_acres)
            self.gcp_points, _ = reject_coords_too_close(self.gcp_points, fam_spacing * min_distance_factor, self.polygon_area_acres)
            self.verification_points, _ = reject_coords_too_close(self.verification_points, fam_spacing * min_distance_factor, self.polygon_area_acres)
            self.logger.debug(f"Post-filtering: {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(self.verification_points)} VCPs generated")

            # Elevation profile with safeguards
            latlon_points = [(p['lat'], p['lon']) for p in self.gcp_points + self.verification_points if p['lat'] is not None and p['lon'] is not None]
            if latlon_points and dsm_path:
                elevation_data['elevations'], elevation_data['cycle_score'], elevation_data['pattern_score'] = get_dsm_elevation_profile(latlon_points, dsm_path, use_dsm=True, pattern_type=layout_mode)
                if not elevation_data['elevations'] or len(elevation_data['elevations']) == 0:
                    self.logger.warning(f"Empty elevation data from DSM: {dsm_path}. Using fallback values.")
                    elevation_data['elevations'] = [291.0] * len(latlon_points)  # From log
                    elevation_data['cycle_score'] = 0.0
                    elevation_data['pattern_score'] = 0.0
                elevation_data['suggested_layout'] = suggest_layout_based_on_dsm(elevation_data['elevations'], area_m2, elevation_data['cycle_score'], elevation_data['pattern_score'])
            else:
                elevation_data['elevations'] = [291.0] * len(self.polygon_coords)
                elevation_data['cycle_score'] = 0.0
                elevation_data['pattern_score'] = 0.0
                elevation_data['suggested_layout'] = layout_mode

            # Compute flight parameters
            self.flight_params = self.compute_flight_parameters(640000, 90.0, 6.0, spacing, self.polygon_area_acres, 80.0, 20.0)
            self.logger.info(f"Flight Parameters: {self.flight_params}")

            self.elevation_data = {
                'min': float(np.min(elevation_data['elevations'])) if elevation_data['elevations'] else 0.0,
                'max': float(np.max(elevation_data['elevations'])) if elevation_data['elevations'] else 0.0,
                'mean': float(np.mean(elevation_data['elevations'])) if elevation_data['elevations'] else 0.0,
                'variance': float(np.var(elevation_data['elevations'], ddof=1)) if len(elevation_data['elevations']) > 1 else 0.0
            }

            self.diagnostic_report = (
                f"Overlay Map Diagnostics ({layout_mode})\n"
                f"• GCP Pattern Score: {unified_detection(len(self.gcp_points), 0):.2f}\n"
                f"• Veri Pattern Score: {unified_detection(len(self.verification_points), 0):.2f}\n"
                f"• Overall Pattern Score: {(elevation_data['pattern_score'] + elevation_data['cycle_score']) / 2:.2f}\n"
                f"• Complexity Rating: {'Low complexity' if (elevation_data['pattern_score'] + elevation_data['cycle_score']) / 2 < 1.0 else 'High complexity'}\n"
                f"→ {elevation_data['suggested_layout']} layout suitable."
            )

            self.logger.info(f"Generated {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(self.verification_points)} verification points, "
                           f"{len(self.rejected_gcp_points)} rejected GCPs, {len(self.rejected_verification_points)} rejected verification points")

            if dem_dataset:
                dem_dataset.close()
            if dsm_dataset:
                dsm_dataset.close()

            return {
                'gcp_points': self.gcp_points,
                'verification_points': self.verification_points,
                'rejected_gcp_points': self.rejected_gcp_points,
                'rejected_verification_points': self.rejected_verification_points,
                'elevation_data': self.elevation_data,
                'flight_params': self.flight_params,
                'diagnostic_report': self.diagnostic_report
            }
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"GCP plan generation failed: {e}")
            if dem_dataset:
                dem_dataset.close()
            if dsm_dataset:
                dsm_dataset.close()
            return {
                'gcp_points': [], 'verification_points': [], 'rejected_gcp_points': [],
                'rejected_verification_points': [], 'elevation_data': {}, 'flight_params': {}, 'diagnostic_report': ''
            }

    def export_to_kmz(self, output_path: str) -> bool:
        """Export GCPs and VCPs to a KMZ file."""
        try:
            kml = Kml()
            for point in self.gcp_points + self.verification_points:
                kml.newpoint(
                    name=point['name'],
                    coords=[(point['lon'], point['lat'])],
                    description=f"{point['type']} | Elev: {point['elevation']:.2f}m"
                )
            kml.savekmz(output_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Exported KMZ to {output_path}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"KMZ export failed: {e}")
            return False

    def run_core_analysis(self) -> Dict:
        """Run core analysis and return current state."""
        start_time = time.time()
        result = {
            'gcp_points': self.gcp_points,
            'verification_points': self.verification_points,
            'rejected_gcp_points': self.rejected_gcp_points,
            'rejected_verification_points': self.rejected_verification_points,
            'elevation_data': self.elevation_data,
            'flight_params': self.flight_params,
            'diagnostic_report': self.diagnostic_report
        }
        self.logger.info(f"Core analysis completed in {time.time() - start_time:.2f}s")
        return result
Thank you for providing the updated MainLogic class from main_logic.py. Key Issues and Objectives
From the log and provided files:

Hardcoded UTM Zones: The provided main_logic.py hardcodes EPSG:32617 in __init__ and uses a manual UTM calculation in load_kmz. Other files like area_utils.py (EPSG:32614), dsm_manager.py (EPSG:32617), kmz_parser.py (EPSG:32614), gcp_generator.py (EPSG:32617), and overlay_generator.py (EPSG:3857) also hardcode CRS, risking misalignment. The log’s coordinates (e.g., (-82.638784, 39.986746)) suggest UTM Zone 17N (EPSG:32617), but all CRS must be auto-detected using get_utm_zone.
Elevation Profile Bug: Log reports min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 despite DSM elevations of 289.0m–322.0m, likely due to issues in max_vegetation_height or generate_gcp_plan in main_logic.py, or dsm_manager.py.
Points Outside DSM Bounds: Points like (1204896.11, -10422451.65) are outside DSM bounds, likely due to incorrect coordinate transformations in kmz_parser.py, dsm_manager.py, or gcp_generator.py.
Rasterio Warning: RuntimeWarning: invalid value encountered in cast in rasterio.transform.py suggests coordinate casting issues in dsm_manager.py or gcp_generator.py.
Performance: Repeated rasterio opens in dsm_manager.py and gcp_generator.py cause overhead.
Complexity Scores: Uniform complexity scores (-0.00) indicate issues with unified_detection in multiple files.
Logging: Files like generate_license_key.py, icon_handler.py, math_utils.py, survey_diagnostics.py, overlay_map_generator.py, terrain_analyzer.py, overlay_generator.py, vegetation_filter.py, and uas_survey_tool.py use print instead of logging with format %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s.
Incomplete File: elevation_service.py is truncated; I’ll reconstruct it.
Math Tool Box: math_tool_box.py is primary; mathtoolbox_complete.py is used in the provided main_logic.py but considered legacy.
Redundant Files: overlay_map.py is a wrapper; uas_survey_tool.py duplicates modern_ui.py.
Installer: UAS_Survey_Tool_Installer.iss references icon.ico instead of app_icon.ico.
UTM Zone Auto-Detection
Using get_utm_zone from utils.py:

Computes centroid longitude of survey area coordinates.
Calculates zone: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Returns EPSG code (e.g., EPSG:32617 for Zone 17N, assuming Northern Hemisphere based on log latitudes ~39°N).
All files handling coordinates must use get_utm_zone or pass utm_crs from callers to avoid hardcoding.

review : import requests
import time
import numpy as np
from math_utils import fibonacci

def detect_elevation_cycles(elevation_data):
    """Detect cyclic patterns in elevation data."""
    fib_mod9 = [1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 4, 3, 7, 1, 8, 0, 8, 8, 7, 6, 4, 1, 5, 6, 2, 8, 1, 0]
    cycle_score = sum(fib_mod9[i % 24] * elev / max(elevation_data + [1]) for i, elev in enumerate(elevation_data)) / len(elevation_data)
    return cycle_score

def get_srtm_elevation_bulk(latlon_points, retry=3, delay=2):
    """
    Queries Open-Elevation or similar public elevation API for a list of lat/lon points.
    Returns list of elevations (in meters) and cycle score.
    """
    api_url = "https://api.opentopodata.org/v1/srtm90m"
    coordinates = [{"latitude": lat, "longitude": lon} for lat, lon in latlon_points]
    elevations = []
    attempt = 0

    while attempt < retry:
        try:
            for i in range(0, len(coordinates), 100):
                chunk = coordinates[i:i + 100]
                response = requests.post(api_url, json={"locations": chunk}, timeout=10)
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    data = response.json()
                    for result in data.get("results", []):
                        elevations.append(result.get("elevation", 0.0))
                else:
                    print(f"[SRTM API] Bad response: {response.status_code}")
                    elevations.extend([0.0] * len(chunk))
                time.sleep(delay)
            cycle_score = detect_elevation_cycles(elevations) if elevations else 0.0
            print(f"[DEBUG] Elevation Cycle Score: {cycle_score:.2f}")
            return elevations, cycle_score
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[SRTM API] Failed: {e}")
            attempt += 1
            if attempt < retry:
                print(f"[INFO] Retrying... Attempt {attempt + 1}/{retry}")
                time.sleep(delay * attempt)
    elevations = [0.0] * len(latlon_points)
    return elevations, 0.0

Review of Provided Code (from dem_downloader.py)
The provided code snippet appears to be part of dem_downloader.py, specifically the get_srtm_elevation_bulk function and its dependency detect_elevation_cycles. Below, I’ll review the code for issues, propose revisions to address the requirements (no hardcoded UTM/CRS, consistent logging, normalized scores, compatibility with UAS Survey Tool v2.0 architecture), and ensure it aligns with the log’s issues (elevation profile bug, points outside DSM bounds, rasterio warning, uniform complexity scores). The revisions will incorporate logging instead of print, normalize detect_elevation_cycles scores, and ensure compatibility with Python 3.9, PyQt6, rasterio, gdal, and styles.qss. I’ll also check for any hardcoded CRS dependencies, although this snippet doesn’t directly handle UTM zones.

Issues Identified
Hardcoded UTM/CRS: The provided code does not explicitly hardcode UTM zones or CRS (e.g., EPSG:32617), which is good. However, it processes latlon_points in WGS84 (EPSG:4326) without transforming them, assuming the API (Open-Elevation) uses WGS84. This is fine for the API but needs verification for integration with other files (e.g., main_logic.py) that expect UTM coordinates.
Elevation Profile Bug: The function returns elevations and cycle_score, but the fallback [0.0] * len(latlon_points) could contribute to the log’s min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 bug if the API fails repeatedly. The detect_elevation_cycles function may also produce negative or zero scores due to unnormalized calculations.
Logging: Uses print statements instead of logging with the format %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s, inconsistent with the project’s logging standard.
Complexity Scores: The cycle_score in detect_elevation_cycles is not normalized, potentially leading to negative or zero values (e.g., log’s -0.00 scores).
Performance: The API call processes coordinates in chunks of 100, which is reasonable, but repeated failures could cause unnecessary retries. No explicit handling of rate limits beyond a fixed delay.
Compatibility: The code is compatible with Python 3.9 and uses requests and numpy, which are in requirements.txt. However, it needs to integrate with main_logic.py and dsm_manager.py for elevation data usage.
Error Handling: Returns [0.0] * len(latlon_points) on failure, which may mask errors and contribute to the elevation profile bug.
Revised Code
Below is the revised code for the provided functions, integrated into a complete dem_downloader.py based on the context of the UAS Survey Tool v2.0. The revisions ensure no hardcoded CRS, use logging, normalize scores, and address the log’s issues.

UTM Zone Auto-Detection
Using get_utm_zone from utils.py:

Computes centroid longitude of survey area coordinates.
Calculates zone: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Returns EPSG code (e.g., EPSG:32617 for Zone 17N, assuming Northern Hemisphere based on log latitudes ~39°N).
All files handling coordinates must use get_utm_zone or pass utm_crs from callers.

# Handle file paths for PyInstaller
def resource_path(relative_path):
    if hasattr(sys, '_MEIPASS'):
        return os.path.join(sys._MEIPASS, relative_path)
    return os.path.join(os.path.abspath("."), relative_path)

class TextEditHandler(logging.Handler):
    def __init__(self, text_edit):
        super().__init__()
        self.text_edit = text_edit

    def emit(self, record):
        msg = self.format(record)
        self.text_edit.append(msg)
        self.text_edit.ensureCursorVisible()

class PointEditorDialog(QDialog):
    def __init__(self, gcp_points, verification_points, polygon_coords, utm_crs, parent=None):
        super().__init__(parent)
        self.setWindowTitle("Point Editor")
        self.gcp_points = gcp_points
        self.verification_points = verification_points
        self.polygon_coords = polygon_coords
        self.utm_crs = utm_crs
        self.selected_points = {'gcp': set(range(len(gcp_points))), 'ver': set(range(len(verification_points)))}
        self.dragging = None
        self.drag_index = None
        self.drag_type = None
        logging.debug(f"PointEditorDialog initialized with polygon_coords: type={type(self.polygon_coords)}, sample={self.polygon_coords[:2] if self.polygon_coords else None}")
        self.init_ui()

    def init_ui(self):
        layout = QVBoxLayout()

        # Matplotlib canvas
        self.fig = Figure(figsize=(8, 6))
        self.canvas = FigureCanvas(self.fig)
        self.ax = self.fig.add_subplot(111)
        layout.addWidget(self.canvas)

        self.plot_points()

        # Point selection lists
        list_layout = QHBoxLayout()
        self.gcp_list = QListWidget()
        self.ver_list = QListWidget()
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f})")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.gcp_list.addItem(item)
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            item = QListWidgetItem(f"{pt['name']} ({pt['easting']:.2f}, {pt['northing']:.2f})")
            item.setFlags(item.flags() | Qt.ItemFlag.ItemIsUserCheckable)
            item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Checked)
            self.ver_list.addItem(item)
        list_layout.addWidget(QLabel("GCPs:"))
        list_layout.addWidget(self.gcp_list)
        list_layout.addWidget(QLabel("Verification Points:"))
        list_layout.addWidget(self.ver_list)
        layout.addLayout(list_layout)

        self.gcp_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)
        self.ver_list.itemChanged.connect(self.update_selection)

        # Matplotlib event handlers
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('button_press_event', self.on_click)
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('motion_notify_event', self.on_motion)
        self.canvas.mpl_connect('button_release_event', self.on_release)

        # Dialog buttons
        buttons = QDialogButtonBox(QDialogButtonBox.StandardButton.Ok | QDialogButtonBox.StandardButton.Cancel)
        buttons.accepted.connect(self.accept)
        buttons.rejected.connect(self.reject)
        layout.addWidget(buttons)

        self.setLayout(layout)

    def plot_points(self):
        self.ax.clear()
        try:
            # Handle polygon_coords as list of dictionaries or tuples
            if self.polygon_coords and isinstance(self.polygon_coords[0], dict):
                x_poly, y_poly = zip(*[(pt['easting'], pt['northing']) for pt in self.polygon_coords])
            elif self.polygon_coords and isinstance(self.polygon_coords[0], tuple):
                x_poly, y_poly = zip(*[(pt[0], pt[1]) for pt in self.polygon_coords])
                logging.debug("Using tuple format for polygon_coords in plot_points")
            else:
                logging.warning("Invalid or empty polygon_coords format, skipping polygon plot")
                x_poly, y_poly = [], []
            self.ax.plot(x_poly + (x_poly[0],), y_poly + (y_poly[0],), 'k-', label="Polygon")
        except Exception as e:
            logging.error(f"Failed to plot polygon: {e}")
            x_poly, y_poly = [], []

        gcp_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        gcp_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points) if i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        ver_x = [pt['easting'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        ver_y = [pt['northing'] for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points) if i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        
        self.gcp_plot = self.ax.scatter(gcp_x, gcp_y, c='blue', marker='o', label="GCPs")
        self.ver_plot = self.ax.scatter(ver_x, ver_y, c='red', marker='x', label="Verification Points")
        
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['gcp']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], pt['name'], fontsize=8, ha='right')
        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            if i in self.selected_points['ver']:
                self.ax.text(pt['easting'], pt['northing'], pt['name'], fontsize=8, ha='left')
        
        self.ax.legend()
        self.ax.set_xlabel("Easting (m)")
        self.ax.set_ylabel("Northing (m)")
        self.ax.set_aspect('equal')
        self.canvas.draw()

    def on_click(self, event):
        if event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        min_dist = float('inf')
        closest_idx = None
        closest_type = None

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.gcp_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'gcp'

        for i, pt in enumerate(self.verification_points):
            dist = np.sqrt((pt['easting'] - x)**2 + (pt['northing'] - y)**2)
            if dist < min_dist and dist < 10:
                min_dist = dist
                closest_idx = i
                closest_type = 'ver'

        if closest_idx is not None:
            if event.button == 1:  # Left click to drag
                self.dragging = True
                self.drag_index = closest_idx
                self.drag_type = closest_type
            elif event.button == 3:  # Right click to toggle
                item = self.gcp_list.item(closest_idx) if closest_type == 'gcp' else self.ver_list.item(closest_idx)
                item.setCheckState(Qt.CheckState.Unchecked if item.checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked else Qt.CheckState.Checked)
                self.update_selection()

    def on_motion(self, event):
        if not self.dragging or event.inaxes != self.ax:
            return
        x, y = event.xdata, event.ydata
        if self.drag_type == 'gcp':
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True).transform(x, y)
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            self.gcp_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.gcp_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        else:
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['easting'] = x
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['northing'] = y
            lon, lat = Transformer.from_crs(self.utm_crs, "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True).transform(x, y)
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lon'] = lon
            self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['lat'] = lat
            self.ver_list.item(self.drag_index).setText(f"{self.verification_points[self.drag_index]['name']} ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f})")
        self.plot_points()

    def on_release(self, event):
        self.dragging = False
        self.drag_index = None
        self.drag_type = None

    def update_selection(self):
        self.selected_points['gcp'] = {i for i in range(self.gcp_list.count()) if self.gcp_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.selected_points['ver'] = {i for i in range(self.ver_list.count()) if self.ver_list.item(i).checkState() == Qt.CheckState.Checked}
        self.plot_points()

    def get_selected_points(self):
        selected_gcp = [self.gcp_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['gcp']]
        selected_ver = [self.verification_points[i] for i in self.selected_points['ver']]
        return selected_gcp, selected_ver

class UASWindow(QMainWindow):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.setWindowTitle("UAS Survey Tool v2.0")
        icon_path = resource_path("app_icon.ico")
        self.setWindowIcon(QIcon(icon_path))
        self.main_logic = MainLogic()
        self.gcp_points = []
        self.verification_points = []
        self.flight_params = {}
        self.area_name = ""
        self.polygon_coords = []
        self.elevation_data = {}
        self.diagnostic_report = ""
        self.kmz_loaded = False
        self.last_kmz_load_time = 0
        self.debounce_interval = 1.0
        self.init_ui()
        self.setup_logging()
        logging.debug("UASWindow instance created")

    def setup_logging(self):
        logging.getLogger().handlers = []
        logging.getLogger(__name__).handlers = []
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.DEBUG, format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s")
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.logger.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        self.logger.propagate = False
        console_handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        console_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        console_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(console_handler)
        log_dir = os.path.expanduser("~/UAS_Survey_Tool_Logs")
        if not os.path.exists(log_dir):
            os.makedirs(log_dir)
        log_path = os.path.join(log_dir, "uas_survey_tool.log")
        file_handler = logging.FileHandler(log_path)
        file_handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        file_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(file_handler)
        handler = TextEditHandler(self.status_log)
        handler.setLevel(logging.DEBUG)
        handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter("%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s"))
        self.logger.addHandler(handler)
        self.logger.debug(f"Logger handlers after setup: {len(self.logger.handlers)}")

    def init_ui(self):
        screen = QApplication.primaryScreen()
        screen_size = screen.availableGeometry()
        screen_width = screen_size.width()
        screen_height = screen_size.height()
        
        min_width = max(800, int(screen_width * 0.7))
        min_height = max(600, int(screen_height * 0.7))
        max_width = min(1400, int(screen_width * 0.9))
        max_height = min(1000, int(screen_height * 0.9))
        self.setMinimumSize(min_width, min_height)
        self.setMaximumSize(max_width, max_height)
        self.resize(min_width, 800)
        logging.debug(f"Screen size: {screen_width}x{screen_height}, "
                     f"Min size: {min_width}x{min_height}, "
                     f"Max size: {max_width}x{max_height}")

        scroll_area = QScrollArea()
        scroll_area.setWidgetResizable(True)
        scroll_area.setStyleSheet("QScrollArea { border: none; background-color: #1e2a44; } "
                                 "QScrollBar:vertical { border: none; background: #2a3f73; width: 10px; margin: 0px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::handle:vertical { background: #3f5ca8; border-radius: 5px; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::add-line:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-line:vertical { background: none; }"
                                 "QScrollBar::add-page:vertical, QScrollBar::sub-page:vertical { background: none; }")
        self.setCentralWidget(scroll_area)

        main_widget = QWidget()
        scroll_area.setWidget(main_widget)
        main_layout = QVBoxLayout(main_widget)
        main_layout.setContentsMargins(10, 10, 10, 10)
        main_layout.setSpacing(15)

        font = QFont("Helvetica", 12)
        self.setFont(font)

        self.setStyleSheet("""
            QMainWindow, QWidget { 
                background-color: #1e2a44; 
                color: #ffffff; 
            }
            QPushButton { 
                background-color: #2a3f73; 
                color: #ffffff; 
                border: 1px solid #3f5ca8; 
                border-radius: 4px; 
                padding: 5px 10px; 
                font-size: 12px; 
            }
            QPushButton#actionButton { 
                background-color: #3f5ca8; 
                font-size: 14px; 
                padding: 8px 15px; 
            }
            QPushButton:hover { 
                background-color: #4a6ad1; 
            }
            QPushButton#actionButton:hover { 
                background-color: #5a7ae1; 
            }
            QLineEdit, QComboBox, QTextEdit, QListWidget { 
                background-color: #354a88; 
                color: #ffffff; 
                border: 1px solid #3f5ca8; 
                border-radius: 4px; 
                padding: 6px; 
            }
            QGroupBox { 
                border: 1px solid #3f5ca8; 
                border-radius: 4px; 
                margin-top: 20px; 
            }
            QGroupBox::title { 
                subcontrol-origin: margin; 
                subcontrol-position: top left; 
                padding: 0 5px; 
                color: #ffffff; 
                font-size: 14px; 
                font-weight: bold; 
            }
        """)

        input_layout.setContentsMargins(10, 20, 10, 10)

            pass

        self.fov_label.setToolTip("Field of View for the LiDAR sensor.")
