        flight_layout.addRow(self.fov_label, self.fov_input)

        self.prr_label = QLabel("Pulse Repetition Rate (kHz):")
        self.prr_label.setToolTip("Pulse rate for RECON-XT LiDAR.")

        flight_layout.addRow(self.prr_label, self.prr_static)

        # Button Row
        button_row = QHBoxLayout()
        self.generate_button = QPushButton("Generate Plan")
        self.generate_button.setObjectName("actionButton")
        self.generate_button.setToolTip("Generate GCP plan and flight parameters.")
        self.generate_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.generate_button.setMinimumWidth(120)
        self.generate_button.setMinimumHeight(35)
        self.generate_button.clicked.connect(self.generate_plan)
        
        self.review_button = QPushButton("Review Points")
        self.review_button.setObjectName("actionButton")

        self.review_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.review_button.setMinimumWidth(120)
        self.review_button.setMinimumHeight(35)
        self.review_button.clicked.connect(self.review_points)
        self.review_button.setEnabled(False)

        self.export_button = QPushButton("Export Deliverables")
        self.export_button.setObjectName("actionButton")
        self.export_button.setToolTip("Export GCPs, verification points, survey plan, report, and overlay map.")
        self.export_button.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed, QSizePolicy.Policy.Fixed)
        self.export_button.setMinimumWidth(120)
        self.export_button.setMinimumHeight(35)
        self.export_button.clicked.connect(self.export_deliverables)
        self.export_button.setEnabled(False)

        button_row.addWidget(self.generate_button)
        button_row.addWidget(self.review_button)
        button_row.addWidget(self.export_button)
        button_row.addStretch()

        log_label = QLabel("Status Log:")
        log_label.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred, QSizePolicy.Policy.Preferred)
        self.status_log = QTextEdit()
        self.status_log.setReadOnly(True)
        self.status_log.setMinimumHeight(200)
        self.status_log.setSizePolicy(QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding, QSizePolicy.Policy.Expanding)

        main_layout.addWidget(input_group)
        main_layout.addWidget(flight_group)
        main_layout.addLayout(button_row)
        main_layout.addWidget(log_label)
        main_layout.addWidget(self.status_log)
        main_layout.addStretch()
        main_layout.setStretch(0, 5)
        main_layout.setStretch(1, 2)
        main_layout.setStretch(2, 1)
        main_layout.setStretch(4, 2)

    def toggle_dem_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dem_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dem_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dem_input.setText("Auto-downloading DEM...")
        else:
            self.dem_input.clear()

    def toggle_dsm_selection(self, state):
        is_checked = state == Qt.CheckState.Checked.value
        self.dsm_input.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        self.dsm_button.setEnabled(not is_checked)
        if is_checked:
            self.dsm_input.setText("Auto-downloading DSM...")
        else:
            self.dsm_input.clear()

    def browse_kmz(self):
        current_time = time.time()
        self.logger.debug(f"browse_kmz called at {current_time}")
        if current_time - self.last_kmz_load_time < self.debounce_interval:
            self.logger.debug("Debounced duplicate call to browse_kmz")
            return
        self.last_kmz_load_time = current_time

        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select KMZ/KML File", "", "KMZ/KML Files (*.kmz *.kml)"
        )
        if file_path and not self.kmz_loaded:
            self.kmz_loaded = True
            self.kmz_input.setText(file_path)
            self.area_name = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(file_path))[0].replace(" ", "_")
            if self.main_logic.load_kmz(file_path):
                area = self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres
                self.polygon_coords = self.main_logic.polygon_coords  # Use dictionary format
                logging.debug(f"Set self.polygon_coords: type={type(self.polygon_coords)}, sample={self.polygon_coords[:2] if self.polygon_coords else None}")
                self.logger.info(f"Loaded KMZ: {file_path}, Area: {area:.2f} acres")
                self.modulus_input.setText(str(self.main_logic.calculate_modulus(area, 26)))
                if self.dem_check.isChecked():
                    self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DEM...")
                    try:
                        dem_path = self.main_logic.download_dem(file_path)
                        self.dem_input.setText(dem_path)
                        self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DEM: {dem_path}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        self.logger.error(f"DEM auto-download failed: {e}")
                        self.dem_check.setChecked(False)
                        self.dem_input.setEnabled(True)
                        self.dem_button.setEnabled(True)
                        self.dem_input.clear()
                else:
                    self.logger.debug("DEM auto-download skipped (checkbox unchecked)")
                if self.dsm_check.isChecked():
                    self.logger.debug("Attempting to download DSM...")
                    try:
                        dsm_path = self.main_logic.download_dsm(file_path)
                        self.dsm_input.setText(dsm_path)
                        self.logger.info(f"Auto-downloaded DSM: {dsm_path}")
                    except Exception as e:
                        self.logger.error(f"DSM auto-download failed: {e}")
                        self.dsm_check.setChecked(False)
                        self.dsm_input.setEnabled(True)
                        self.dsm_button.setEnabled(True)
                        self.dsm_input.clear()
                else:
                    self.logger.debug("DSM auto-download skipped (checkbox unchecked)")
            else:
                self.logger.error("Failed to load KMZ file.")
        elif file_path:
            self.logger.debug("KMZ file already loaded, skipping duplicate processing.")

    def browse_dem(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DEM File", "", "DEM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dem_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DEM: {file_path}")

    def browse_dsm(self):
        file_path, _ = QFileDialog.getOpenFileName(
            self, "Select DSM File", "", "DEM Files (*.tif *.tiff)"
        )
        if file_path:
            self.dsm_input.setText(file_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Selected DSM: {file_path}")

    def update_sequence(self):
        sequence_type = self.sequence_combo.currentText()
        modulus = self.modulus_input.text()
        modulus = int(modulus) if modulus.isdigit() else None
        self.main_logic.set_sequence_type(sequence_type, modulus)

    def generate_plan(self):
        self.logger.debug("Starting plan generation")
        try:
            self.kmz_loaded = False
            spacing = int(self.spacing_combo.currentText())
            layout_mode = self.layout_combo.currentText()
            self.logger.debug(f"Selected layout mode: {layout_mode}")
            dem_path = self.dem_input.text() if self.dem_input.text() else None
            dsm_path = self.dsm_input.text() if self.dsm_input.text() else None
            accuracy = float(self.accuracy_input.text()) if self.accuracy_input.text() else 6.0
            altitude = float(self.altitude_input.text()) if self.altitude_input.text() else 80.0
            fov = float(self.fov_input.text()) if self.fov_input.text() else 90.0
            prr = 640000

            self.logger.debug("Generating GCP plan...")
            self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, self.elevation_data = self.main_logic.generate_gcp_plan(spacing, layout_mode, dem_path, dsm_path)
            self.diagnostic_report = generate_overlay_diagnostics(self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, layout_mode)
            self.logger.info(f"Generated {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs and {len(self.verification_points)} verification points.")
            self.logger.info(f"Overlay Diagnostics: {self.diagnostic_report}")

            self.flight_params = self.main_logic.compute_flight_parameters(accuracy, altitude, fov, prr)
            if self.flight_params:
                self.logger.info(
                    f"Flight Parameters: Accuracy={self.flight_params['accuracy']}mm, Altitude={self.flight_params['altitude']}m, "
                    f"FOV={self.flight_params['fov']}deg, PRR={self.flight_params['prr']/1000}kHz, Speed={self.flight_params['speed']}m/s, "
                    f"Resolution={self.flight_params['resolution']:.2f}cm/pixel"
                )
            else:
                self.logger.error("Failed to compute flight parameters.")
            
            self.review_button.setEnabled(True)
            self.export_button.setEnabled(False)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Plan generation failed: {str(e)}")

    def review_points(self):
        try:
            dialog = PointEditorDialog(self.gcp_points, self.verification_points, self.main_logic.polygon_coords, self.main_logic.utm_crs, self)
            if dialog.exec():
                self.gcp_points, self.verification_points = dialog.get_selected_points()
                self.logger.info(f"Selected {len(self.gcp_points)} GCPs and {len(self.verification_points)} verification points.")
                self.export_button.setEnabled(True)
            else:
                self.logger.info("Point review cancelled.")
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to open point editor: {e}")

    def export_deliverables(self):
        try:
            if not self.gcp_points or not self.flight_params:
                self.logger.warning("Incomplete plan generated. Exporting available data.")
            export_dir = QFileDialog.getExistingDirectory(self, "Select Export Folder")
            if not export_dir:
                self.logger.error("No export folder selected.")
                return

            date_str = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
            area_prefix = self.area_name or "Survey"
            gcp_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_GCPs.csv"
            ver_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_VerificationPoints.csv"
            kmz_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_SurveyPlan.kmz"
            report_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_SurveyReport.pdf"
            overlay_filename = f"{area_prefix}_{date_str}_OverlayMap.png"

            fields = ['name', 'lat', 'lon', 'elevation', 'easting', 'northing', 'pattern_score', 'global_offset']

            if self.gcp_points:
                gcp_csv_path = os.path.join(export_dir, gcp_filename)
                with open(gcp_csv_path, 'w', newline='') as csvfile:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fields)
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for point in self.gcp_points:
                        writer.writerow(point)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported GCPs to {gcp_csv_path}")

            if self.verification_points:
                ver_csv_path = os.path.join(export_dir, ver_filename)
                with open(ver_csv_path, 'w', newline='') as csvfile:
                    writer = csv.DictWriter(csvfile, fieldnames=fields)
                    writer.writeheader()
                    for point in self.verification_points:
                        writer.writerow(point)
                self.logger.info(f"Exported verification points to {ver_csv_path}")

            if self.gcp_points or self.verification_points:
                try:
                    kml = simplekml.Kml()
                    if self.gcp_points:
                        control_folder = kml.newfolder(name="GCPs")
                        for point in self.gcp_points:
                            pnt = control_folder.newpoint(name=point['name'])
                            pnt.coords = [(point['lon'], point['lat'], point['elevation'])]
                            pnt.description = f"Pattern Score: {point['pattern_score']:.2f}"
                    if self.verification_points:
                        verification_folder = kml.newfolder(name="Verification Points")
                        for point in self.verification_points:
                            pnt = verification_folder.newpoint(name=point['name'])
                            pnt.coords = [(point['lon'], point['lat'], point['elevation'])]
                            pnt.description = f"Pattern Score: {point['pattern_score']:.2f}"
                    kml_path = os.path.join(export_dir, "survey_plan.kml")
                    kml.save(kml_path)
                    kmz_path = os.path.join(export_dir, kmz_filename)
                    with zipfile.ZipFile(kmz_path, 'w', compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as kmz:
                        kmz.write(kml_path, 'doc.kml')
                    os.remove(kml_path)
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported survey plan to {kmz_path}")
                except ImportError:
                    self.logger.error("KMZ export requires 'simplekml'. Install it with 'pip install simplekml'.")
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.error(f"KMZ export failed: {e}")

            if self.gcp_points or self.verification_points:
                try:
                    overlay_path = os.path.join(export_dir, overlay_filename)
                    generate_overlay_map(
                        gcp_points=[{k: p[k] for k in ['easting', 'northing']} for p in self.gcp_points],
                        verification_points=[{k: p[k] for k in ['easting', 'northing']} for p in self.verification_points],
                        polygon_coords=self.main_logic.polygon_utm.exterior.coords if self.main_logic.polygon_utm else [],
                        output_path=overlay_path
                    )
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported overlay map to {overlay_path}")

                    report_path = os.path.join(export_dir, report_filename)
                    dsm_summary = (
                        f"Elevation Range: {self.elevation_data.get('min', 0):.2f}m to {self.elevation_data.get('max', 0):.2f}m\n"
                        f"Mean Elevation: {self.elevation_data.get('mean', 0):.2f}m\n"
                        f"Diagnostics: {self.diagnostic_report}"
                    )
                    generate_report(
                        output_path=report_path,
                        polygon_coords=self.polygon_coords,
                        gcp_points=self.gcp_points,
                        veri_points=self.verification_points,
                        spacing=int(self.spacing_combo.currentText()),
                        layout_mode=self.layout_combo.currentText(),
                        area_acres=self.main_logic.polygon_area_acres,
                        elevation_data=self.elevation_data,
                        dsm_summary=dsm_summary,
                        overlay_image_path=overlay_path,
                        flight_timings=None,
                        pattern_score=self.gcp_points[0]['pattern_score'] if self.gcp_points else 0.0
                    )
                    self.logger.info(f"Exported report to {report_path}")
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.error(f"Report/overlay export failed: {e}")

        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Export failed: {str(e)}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = QApplication(sys.argv)
    app.setAttribute(Qt.AA_EnableHighDpiScaling)
    app.setAttribute(Qt.AA_UseHighDpiPixmaps)
    app.setStyle('Fusion')
    window = UASWindow()
    window.show()
    sys.exit(app.exec())

Key Issues and Objectives
From the log and provided files:

Hardcoded UTM Zones: The provided main_logic.py hardcodes EPSG:32617 in __init__ and uses manual UTM calculation in load_kmz. Other files (area_utils.py: EPSG:32614, dsm_manager.py: EPSG:32617, kmz_parser.py: EPSG:32614, gcp_generator.py: EPSG:32617, overlay_generator.py: EPSG:3857) also hardcode CRS. The log’s coordinates (e.g., (-82.638784, 39.986746)) suggest UTM Zone 17N (EPSG:32617), but all CRS must use get_utm_zone from utils.py.
Elevation Profile Bug: Log reports min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 despite DSM elevations of 289.0m–322.0m, likely due to issues in main_logic.py (max_vegetation_height, generate_gcp_plan) or elevation_service.py (get_srtm_elevation_bulk).

Rasterio Warning: RuntimeWarning: invalid value encountered in cast in rasterio.transform.py suggests issues in dsm_manager.py or gcp_generator.py.

Complexity Scores: Uniform -0.00 scores indicate issues with unified_detection (in math_utils.py) or detect_elevation_cycles (in elevation_service.py).
Logging: The provided modern_ui.py uses proper logging, but other files (e.g., generate_license_key.py, icon_handler.py) use print instead of logging with %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s.
Math Tool Box: math_tool_box.py is primary; mathtoolbox_complete.py is legacy but used in main_logic.py.

UTM Zone Auto-Detection
Using get_utm_zone from utils.py:

Computes centroid longitude of survey area coordinates.
Calculates zone: zone = floor((longitude + 180) / 6) + 1.
Returns EPSG code (e.g., EPSG:32617 for Zone 17N, assuming Northern Hemisphere based on log latitudes ~39°N).
All files handling coordinates must use get_utm_zone or pass utm_crs from callers.

import zipfile
import tempfile
import logging
import shutil
from pykml import parser
from simplekml import Kml
from shapely.geometry import Polygon, LineString
import numpy as np
from pyproj import Transformer

try:
    from fastkml import kml as fastkml
except ImportError:
    fastkml = None

def fibonacci(n):
    fib = [0, 1]
    for i in range(2, n+1):
        fib.append(fib[i-1] + fib[i-2])
    return fib

def unified_detection(k, t, weights=[0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25], T=24):
    """FAM Comprehensive Sequence Detection for pattern scoring."""
    try:
        fib = fibonacci(max(2*k, k+1))
        fib_mod9 = [1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 4, 3, 7, 1, 8, 0, 8, 8, 7, 6, 4, 1, 5, 6, 2, 8, 1, 0]
        logistic = [0.1, 0.2]
        for _ in range(k-1):
            logistic.append((logistic[-1] + logistic[-2]) % 1)
        max_fib = max(fib) if fib else 1
        recursive = fib[k] / max_fib if max_fib != 0 else 0
        cyclic = fib_mod9[k % 24]
        fractal = fib[2 * fib[k] - 2] / max_fib if 2 * fib[k] - 2 < len(fib) else 0
        chaotic = logistic[k]
        score = (weights[0] * recursive + weights[1] * cyclic + weights[2] * fractal +
                 weights[3] * chaotic) * (1 + np.cos(2 * np.pi * t / T))
        return min(max(score * 10, 4.0), 10.0)  # Scale to ~4-10
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Pattern score calculation failed: {e}")
        return 4.0

def extract_kml_from_kmz(kmz_path):
    """Extract KML file from KMZ archive or return KML file path directly."""
    try:
        _, ext = os.path.splitext(kmz_path)
        ext = ext.lower()
        
        if ext == '.kml':
            logging.debug(f"Input is a KML file: {kmz_path}")
            return kmz_path, None
        
        elif ext == '.kmz':
            temp_dir = tempfile.mkdtemp()
            with zipfile.ZipFile(kmz_path, 'r') as zip_ref:
                zip_ref.extractall(temp_dir)
            for root, _, files in os.walk(temp_dir):
                for file in files:
                    if file.endswith('.kml'):
                        kml_path = os.path.join(root, file)
                        logging.debug(f"Extracted KML from KMZ: {kml_path}")
                        return kml_path, temp_dir
            raise ValueError("No KML file found in KMZ archive")
        
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported file extension: {ext}. Expected .kmz or .kml")
    
    except zipfile.BadZipFile:
        logging.error(f"File is not a valid zip file: {kmz_path}")
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"KML extraction failed: {e}")
        raise

def parse_kml_geometry_pykml(kml_file):
    """Parse geometries from KML file using pykml."""
    try:
        logging.debug("Attempting pykml parser")
        with open(kml_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            kml_content = f.read()
            logging.debug(f"KML content preview (first 500 chars): {kml_content[:500]}...")
            kml_doc = parser.fromstring(kml_content.encode('utf-8'))
        
        geometries = []
        # Transformer for UTM (Zone 14N, EPSG:32614) to WGS84 (EPSG:4326)
        transformer = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:32614", "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        
        def process_element(element, parent_name=""):
            for placemark in element.findall('.//{http://www.opengis.net/kml/2.2}Placemark'):
                name = getattr(placemark, 'name', parent_name) or f"Placemark_{len(geometries)}"
                logging.debug(f"Processing placemark: {name}")
                
                if hasattr(placemark, 'Polygon'):
                    polygon = placemark.Polygon
                    if hasattr(polygon, 'outerBoundaryIs'):
                        coords_str = polygon.outerBoundaryIs.LinearRing.coordinates.text.strip()
                        coords = []
                        for coord in coords_str.split():
                            try:
                                parts = coord.split(',')
                                if len(parts) < 2:
                                    logging.warning(f"Invalid coordinate format in {name}: {coord}")
                                    continue
                                lon, lat, *rest = parts
                                try:
                                    lon = float(lon)
                                    lat = float(lat)
                                    # Check if coordinates are likely UTM (large values)
                                    if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                                        logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                        lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                                        logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                except (ValueError, OverflowError) as e:
                                    logging.warning(f"Invalid coordinate value in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}, error: {e}")
                                    continue
                                if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                                    logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                    continue
                                coords.append((lon, lat))
                            except Exception as e:
                                logging.warning(f"Failed to parse coordinate in {name}: {coord}, error: {e}")
                                continue
                        if len(coords) >= 3:
                            geom = Polygon(coords)
                            pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                            geometries.append({
                                "name": name,
                                "geometry": geom,
                                "coords": coords,
                                "pattern_score": pattern_score
                            })
                            logging.debug(f"Found Polygon: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
                
                if hasattr(placemark, 'LineString'):
                    linestring = placemark.LineString
                    coords_str = linestring.coordinates.text.strip()
                    coords = []
                    for coord in coords_str.split():
                        try:
                            parts = coord.split(',')
                            if len(parts) < 2:
                                logging.warning(f"Invalid coordinate format in {name}: {coord}")
                                continue
                            lon, lat, *rest = parts
                            try:
                                lon = float(lon)
                                lat = float(lat)
                                if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                                    logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                    lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                                    logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            except (ValueError, OverflowError) as e:
                                logging.warning(f"Invalid coordinate value in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}, error: {e}")
                                continue
                            if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                                logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                continue
                            coords.append((lon, lat))
                        except Exception as e:
                            logging.warning(f"Failed to parse coordinate in {name}: {coord}, error: {e}")
                            continue
                    if len(coords) >= 2:
                        geom = LineString(coords)
                        pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                        geometries.append({
                            "name": name,
                            "geometry": geom,
                            "coords": coords,
                            "pattern_score": pattern_score
                        })
                        logging.debug(f"Found LineString: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
        
        for doc in kml_doc.findall('.//{http://www.opengis.net/kml/2.2}Document'):
            doc_name = getattr(doc, 'name', 'Unnamed')
            logging.debug(f"Processing document: {doc_name}")
            process_element(doc, doc_name)
        
        if not geometries:
            logging.warning("No valid Polygon or LineString geometries found in KML with pykml")
            raise ValueError("No valid geometries found in KML")
        
        return geometries
    
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"pykml parsing failed: {e}")
        raise

def parse_kml_geometry_simplekml(kml_file):
    """Parse geometries from KML file using simplekml."""
    try:
        logging.debug("Attempting simplekml parser")
        kml = Kml()
        kml.from_string(open(kml_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8').read())
        
        geometries = []
        transformer = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:32614", "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        
        def process_features(features, parent_name=""):
            for feature in features:
                name = feature.name or f"Feature_{len(geometries)}"
                if hasattr(feature, 'geometry'):
                    geom = feature.geometry
                    if geom.type == 'Polygon':
                        coords = []
                        for pt in geom.exteriorpoints:
                            lon, lat = pt.coords[0][0], pt.coords[0][1]
                            if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                                logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                                logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                                logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                continue
                            coords.append((lon, lat))
                        if len(coords) >= 3:
                            shapely_geom = Polygon(coords)
                            pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                            geometries.append({
                                "name": name,
                                "geometry": shapely_geom,
                                "coords": coords,
                                "pattern_score": pattern_score
                            })
                            logging.debug(f"Found Polygon: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
                    elif geom.type == 'LineString':
                        coords = []
                        for pt in geom.points:
                            lon, lat = pt.coords[0][0], pt.coords[0][1]
                            if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                                logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                                logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                                logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                                continue
                            coords.append((lon, lat))
                        if len(coords) >= 2:
                            shapely_geom = LineString(coords)
                            pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                            geometries.append({
                                "name": name,
                                "geometry": shapely_geom,
                                "coords": coords,
                                "pattern_score": pattern_score
                            })
                            logging.debug(f"Found LineString: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
                if hasattr(feature, 'features'):
                    process_features(feature.features(), name)
        
        process_features(kml.features())
        
        if not geometries:
            logging.warning("No valid Polygon or LineString geometries found in KML with simplekml")
            raise ValueError("No valid geometries found in KML")
        
        return geometries
    
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"simplekml parsing failed: {e}")
        raise

def parse_kml_geometry_fastkml(kml_file):
    """Parse geometries from KML file using fastkml, if available."""
    if not fastkml:
        logging.warning("fastkml not installed, skipping fastkml parser")
        raise ValueError("fastkml not available")
    
    try:
        logging.debug("Attempting fastkml parser")
        with open(kml_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            kml_content = f.read()
            k = fastkml.KML()
            k.from_string(kml_content.encode('utf-8'))
        
        geometries = []
        transformer = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:32614", "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        
        def process_features(features, parent_name=""):
            for feature in features:
                name = feature.name or f"Feature_{len(geometries)}"
                if isinstance(feature, fastkml.geometry.Polygon):
                    coords = []
                    for pt in feature.exterior:
                        lon, lat = pt[0], pt[1]
                        if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                            logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                            logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                        if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                            logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            continue
                        coords.append((lon, lat))
                    if len(coords) >= 3:
                        geom = Polygon(coords)
                        pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                        geometries.append({
                            "name": name,
                            "geometry": geom,
                            "coords": coords,
                            "pattern_score": pattern_score
                        })
                        logging.debug(f"Found Polygon: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
                elif isinstance(feature, fastkml.geometry.LineString):
                    coords = []
                    for pt in feature.coordinates:
                        lon, lat = pt[0], pt[1]
                        if abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90:
                            logging.debug(f"Attempting UTM conversion for {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            lon, lat = transformer.transform(lon, lat)
                            logging.debug(f"Converted to WGS84: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                        if not (-180 <= lon <= 180 and -90 <= lat <= 90):
                            logging.warning(f"Coordinate out of WGS84 range in {name}: lon={lon}, lat={lat}")
                            continue
                        coords.append((lon, lat))
                    if len(coords) >= 2:
                        geom = LineString(coords)
                        pattern_score = unified_detection(len(coords), 0)
                        geometries.append({
                            "name": name,
                            "geometry": geom,
                            "coords": coords,
                            "pattern_score": pattern_score
                        })
                        logging.debug(f"Found LineString: {name}, Pattern Score: {pattern_score:.2f}")
                if hasattr(feature, 'features'):
                    process_features(feature.features(), name)
        
        for doc in k.features:
            process_features(doc.features, doc.name or "Unnamed")
        
        if not geometries:
            logging.warning("No valid Polygon or LineString geometries found in KML with fastkml")
            raise ValueError("No valid geometries found in KML")
        
        return geometries
    
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"fastkml parsing failed: {e}")
        raise

def parse_kml_geometry(kml_file):
    """Parse geometries from KML file, trying multiple parsers."""
    parsers = [
        ("pykml", parse_kml_geometry_pykml),
        ("simplekml", parse_kml_geometry_simplekml),
        ("fastkml", parse_kml_geometry_fastkml)
    ]
    
    for parser_name, parser_func in parsers:
        try:
            return parser_func(kml_file)
        except Exception as e:
            logging.warning(f"Parser {parser_name} failed, trying next parser: {e}")
    
    logging.error("All parsers failed to extract geometries")
    raise ValueError("No valid geometries found in KML after trying all parsers")

def extract_polygon_from_kmz(kmz_path):
    """Extract first polygon coordinates from KMZ or KML file."""
    try:
        kml_file, temp_dir = extract_kml_from_kmz(kmz_path)
        try:
            geometries = parse_kml_geometry(kml_file)
            for geom in geometries:
                if isinstance(geom['geometry'], Polygon):
                    logging.debug(f"Extracted polygon: {geom['name']}, Pattern Score: {geom['pattern_score']:.2f}")
                    return geom['coords']
            raise ValueError("No polygon geometry found in KMZ/KML")
        finally:
            if temp_dir and os.path.exists(temp_dir):
                try:
                    shutil.rmtree(temp_dir)
                    logging.debug(f"Cleaned up temporary directory: {temp_dir}")
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.warning(f"Failed to clean up temporary directory {temp_dir}: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Polygon extraction failed: {e}")
        raise

def extract_geometries_from_kmz(kmz_path):
    """Extract all geometries from KMZ or KML file."""
    try:
        kml_file, temp_dir = extract_kml_from_kmz(kmz_path)
        try:
            return parse_kml_geometry(kml_file)
        finally:
            if temp_dir and os.path.exists(temp_dir):
                try:
                    shutil.rmtree(temp_dir)
                    logging.debug(f"Cleaned up temporary directory: {temp_dir}")
                except Exception as e:
                    logging.warning(f"Failed to clean up temporary directory {temp_dir}: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"Geometry extraction failed: {e}")
        raise

Analysis of kmz_parser.py (Older Version)
Strengths of the Older Version:

Multiple Parsers: Uses pykml, simplekml, and fastkml (if available), providing robust fallback parsing for KML files, increasing compatibility with various KML formats.
UTM Detection Fallback: Detects potential UTM coordinates (abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90) and transforms them from EPSG:32614 to EPSG:4326, preventing coordinate misinterpretation.
Pattern Scoring: Integrates unified_detection for geometry scoring, aligning with the tool’s sequence-based surveying.
Temporary Directory Cleanup: Uses tempfile.mkdtemp and shutil.rmtree for robust cleanup of extracted KML files.
Logging: Uses logging with detailed debug and warning messages, though not in the exact %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s format.
Error Handling: Gracefully handles invalid coordinates, bad zip files, and parser failures.
Issues in the Older Version:

Hardcoded CRS: Assumes EPSG:32614 (UTM Zone 14N) for coordinate transformation, which fails for areas outside this zone (e.g., log’s coordinates (-82.638784, 39.986746) suggest Zone 17N, EPSG:32617).
Points Outside DSM Bounds: The hardcoded EPSG:32614 likely caused incorrect transformations, leading to points like (1204896.11, -10422451.65) being outside DSM bounds.
Complexity Scores: unified_detection may produce negative or low scores (contributing to log’s -0.00), as it lacks normalization to ensure positive values.
Logging Format: Missing the exact %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s format.
Dependency on fastkml: Optional fastkml import may cause inconsistencies if unavailable.
Why It Worked Well:

The multiple-parser approach (pykml, simplekml, fastkml) ensured robustness across different KML/KMZ formats, reducing parsing failures.
The UTM detection heuristic (abs(lon) > 180 or abs(lat) > 90) caught misprojected coordinates, though it used a hardcoded CRS.
Comprehensive logging helped debug issues, making it easier to identify problems during development.
Why Recent Revisions May Have Broken It:

Recent versions (e.g., from earlier responses) removed simplekml and fastkml, relying solely on pykml, which may fail on complex or non-standard KML files.
Removed the UTM detection heuristic, assuming WGS84 input, which could fail if the input KML contains UTM coordinates.
Simplified error handling may have reduced robustness.
Key Issues and Objectives
From the log and provided files:

Hardcoded UTM Zones: The older kmz_parser.py hardcodes EPSG:32614; main_logic.py hardcodes EPSG:32617. Other files (area_utils.py: EPSG:32614, dsm_manager.py: EPSG:32617, gcp_generator.py: EPSG:32617, overlay_generator.py: EPSG:3857) also hardcode CRS. All must use get_utm_zone.
Elevation Profile Bug: Log’s min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 likely from elevation_service.py’s get_srtm_elevation_bulk or main_logic.py’s max_vegetation_height.
Points Outside DSM Bounds: Likely due to incorrect transformations in kmz_parser.py, main_logic.py, or dsm_manager.py.
Rasterio Warning: RuntimeWarning: invalid value encountered in cast suggests issues in dsm_manager.py or gcp_generator.py.
Performance: Repeated rasterio opens; API retries in elevation_service.py.
Complexity Scores: Uniform -0.00 scores from unnormalized unified_detection or detect_elevation_cycles.
Logging: Some files use print instead of logging with %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s.
Math Tool Box: math_tool_box.py is primary; mathtoolbox_complete.py is legacy.
Redundant Files: overlay_map.py is a wrapper; uas_survey_tool.py duplicates modern_ui.py.
Installer: UAS_Survey_Tool_Installer.iss references icon.ico instead of app_icon.ico.
UI/UX Preferences: Retain modern_ui.py’s theme (dark blue #1e2a44, button #3f5ca8), spacing (10–20px), and PointEditorDialog without rejected points initially, but add rejected points for completeness.

import numpy as np
from pyproj import Transformer
import math
import rasterio
from rasterio.transform import rowcol
from flight_parameters_calculator import compute_flight_parameters
from dsm_manager import get_dsm_elevation_profile
from filter_coordinates import reject_coords_too_close
from area_utils import calculate_area_acres

def fibonacci(n):
    fib = [0, 1]
    for i in range(2, n+1):
        fib.append(fib[i-1] + fib[i-2])
    return fib

def unified_detection(k, t, weights=[0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25], T=24):
    """FAM Comprehensive Sequence Detection for pattern scoring."""
    fib = fibonacci(max(2*k, k+1))
    fib_mod9 = [1, 1, 2, 3, 5, 8, 4, 3, 7, 1, 8, 0, 8, 8, 7, 6, 4, 1, 5, 6, 2, 8, 1, 0]
    x = [0.1, 0.2] + [(x[-1] + x[-2]) % 1 for _ in range(k-1)]  # Fibonacci logistic map
    recursive = fib[k]
    cyclic = fib_mod9[k % 24]
    fractal = fib[2 * fib[k] - 2] if 2 * fib[k] - 2 < len(fib) else 0
    chaotic = x[k]
    return (weights[0] * recursive + weights[1] * cyclic + weights[2] * fractal +
            weights[3] * chaotic) * (1 + np.cos(2 * np.pi * t / T))

def calculate_fam_spacing(area_acres, base_spacing):
    """Calculate FAM-based spacing using survey area."""
    fib = fibonacci(20)
    index = int(np.log(area_acres + 1) * 2)
    index = min(max(index, 2), len(fib)-1)
    return base_spacing * fib[index] / fib[5]  # Normalize relative to F_5 = 5

def calculate_gcp_spacing(area_acres, flight_params):
    """Calculate GCP spacing using flight parameters."""
    print(f"[DEBUG] Calculating GCP spacing for area={area_acres:.2f} acres")
    params = compute_flight_parameters(
        area_acres=area_acres,
        altitude_m=flight_params['agl'],
        speed_mps=flight_params['speed'],
        pulse_rate_pps=flight_params['pulse_rate'],
        fov_deg=flight_params['fov_deg'],
        accuracy_mm=flight_params['accuracy_mm'],
        spacing_m=flight_params['spacing']
    )
    spacing = min(max(params['recommended_spacing_m'], 300), 500)
    n_gcps = params['estimated_gcp_count']
    print(f"[DEBUG] Calculated {n_gcps} GCPs, spacing={spacing:.2f}m")
    return spacing, n_gcps

def is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer_to_utm):
    """Check if a point avoids vegetation (DSM-DEM > 2m) and water (low DEM)."""
    try:
        lon, lat = transformer_to_utm.invert(x, y)
        row, col = rowcol(dem_dataset.transform, lon, lat)
        if not (0 <= row < dem_dataset.height and 0 <= col < dem_dataset.width):
            return False, "Outside raster bounds"
        
        dem_value = list(dem_dataset.sample([(lon, lat)]))[0][0]
        dsm_value = list(dsm_dataset.sample([(lon, lat)]))[0][0]
        
        veg_height = dsm_value - dem_value
        if veg_height > 2.0:
            return False, "Heavy vegetation"
        
        min_elevation = np.min(list(dem_dataset.sample([(lon, lat) for lon, lat in [(lon, lat)]])))
        if dem_value < min_elevation + 5.0:
            return False, "Water body"
        
        return True, "Suitable"
    except Exception as e:
        return False, f"Raster sampling failed: {e}"

def generate_fractal_gcp_layout(polygon, spacing, area_acres):
    """Generate GCPs using fractal-like Fibonacci placement."""
    fib = fibonacci(20)
    minx, miny, maxx, maxy = polygon.bounds
    points = []
    for k in range(3, 10):  # Fibonacci indices F_3 to F_9
        fk = fib[k]
        scale = spacing * fk / fib[5]
        for i in range(int(area_acres / fk)):
            x = minx + (maxx - minx) * (i % fk) / fk
            y = miny + (maxy - miny) * (i // fk) / fk
            point = Point(x, y)
            if polygon.contains(point):
                pattern_score = unified_detection(k, 0)
                points.append({'lat': y, 'lon': x, 'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': pattern_score})
    return points

def generate_chaotic_gcp_layout(polygon, n_gcps, spacing, area_acres):
    """Generate chaotic GCPs with predictive adjustments."""
    minx, miny, maxx, maxy = polygon.bounds
    points = []
    attempts = 0
    max_attempts = n_gcps * 10
    k = int(np.log(area_acres + 1) * 2)
    chaos_factor = unified_detection(k, 0, weights=[0.1, 0.1, 0.4, 0.4])
    adjusted_spacing = spacing * (1 + chaos_factor / 10)
    while len(points) < n_gcps and attempts < max_attempts:
        x = np.random.uniform(minx, maxx)
        y = np.random.uniform(miny, maxy)
        if polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
            pattern_score = unified_detection(len(points), 0)
            points.append({'lat': y, 'lon': x, 'easting': x, 'northing': y, 'pattern_score': pattern_score})
        attempts += 1
    return points

def generate_gcps_within_polygon(polygon_coords, spacing, layout_mode="grid", flight_params=None, dem_path=None, dsm_path=None):
    """Generate GCPs and verification points, avoiding vegetation/water."""
    print(f"[DEBUG] Generating GCPs: spacing={spacing}m, mode={layout_mode}, dem={dem_path}, dsm={dsm_path}")
    try:
        if not flight_params:
            raise ValueError("Flight parameters required")
        if not dem_path or not dsm_path:
            print("[WARNING] DEM/DSM not provided; skipping terrain filtering")
        
        # Create Shapely Polygon
        polygon = Polygon(polygon_coords)
        if not polygon.is_valid:
            raise ValueError("Invalid polygon geometry")
        
        # Transform to UTM
        transformer_to_utm = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:4326", "EPSG:32614", always_xy=True)
        transformer_to_wgs84 = Transformer.from_crs("EPSG:32614", "EPSG:4326", always_xy=True)
        utm_coords = [transformer_to_utm.transform(lon, lat) for lon, lat in polygon_coords]
        utm_polygon = Polygon(utm_coords)
        area_m2, area_acres, fam_scale, _ = calculate_area_acres(polygon_coords)
        
        # Calculate spacing
        spacing_meters, n_gcps = calculate_gcp_spacing(area_acres, flight_params)
        fam_spacing = calculate_fam_spacing(area_acres, spacing_meters)
        print(f"[DEBUG] FAM-adjusted spacing: {fam_spacing:.2f}m")
        
        # Load DEM/DSM
        dem_dataset = rasterio.open(dem_path) if dem_path else None
        dsm_dataset = rasterio.open(dsm_path) if dsm_path else None
        
        # Generate points
        minx, miny, maxx, maxy = utm_polygon.bounds
        print(f"[DEBUG] UTM bounds: minx={minx:.2f}, miny={miny:.2f}, maxx={maxx:.2f}, maxy={maxy:.2f}")
        
        gcp_points = []
        if layout_mode == "grid":
            x = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing)
            y = np.arange(miny, maxy, fam_spacing)
            if len(x) == 0 or len(y) == 0:
                raise ValueError("Grid generation failed")
            xv, yv = np.meshgrid(x, y)
            points = np.vstack((xv.ravel(), yv.ravel())).T
        elif layout_mode == "triangular":
            x = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing)
            y = np.arange(miny, maxy, fam_spacing * np.sqrt(3)/2)
            points = []
            for i, y_val in enumerate(y):
                x_offset = (fam_spacing / 2) if i % 2 else 0
                for x_val in x:
                    points.append([x_val + x_offset, y_val])
            points = np.array(points)
        elif layout_mode == "diamond":
            x = np.arange(minx, maxx, fam_spacing)
            y = np.arange(miny, maxy, fam_spacing)
            xv, yv = np.meshgrid(x, y)
            points = np.vstack((xv.ravel(), yv.ravel())).T
            theta = np.pi / 4
            rot_matrix = np.array([[np.cos(theta), -np.sin(theta)], [np.sin(theta), np.cos(theta)]])
            points = points @ rot_matrix
        elif layout_mode == "spiral":
            centroid = utm_polygon.centroid
            r_max = max(np.sqrt((maxx - minx)**2 + (maxy - miny)**2)) / 2
            points = []
            for i in range(n_gcps * 2):
                theta = i * 2 * np.pi / n_gcps
                r = (i / n_gcps) * r_max
                x = centroid.x + r * np.cos(theta)
                y = centroid.y + r * np.sin(theta)
                points.append([x, y])
            points = np.array(points)
        elif layout_mode == "chaotic":
            gcp_points = generate_chaotic_gcp_layout(utm_polygon, n_gcps, fam_spacing, area_acres)
            points = np.array([[p['easting'], p['northing']] for p in gcp_points])
        elif layout_mode == "fibonacci":
            centroid = utm_polygon.centroid
            points = []
            n = max(n_gcps, 10)
            golden_angle = np.pi * (3 - np.sqrt(5))
            for i in range(n * 2):
                theta = golden_angle * i
                r = fam_spacing * np.sqrt(i / n)
                x = centroid.x + r * np.cos(theta)
                y = centroid.y + r * np.sin(theta)
                if utm_polygon.contains(Point(x, y)):
                    points.append([x, y])
            points = np.array(points)
        elif layout_mode == "fractal":
            gcp_points = generate_fractal_gcp_layout(utm_polygon, fam_spacing, area_acres)
            points = np.array([[p['easting'], p['northing']] for p in gcp_points])
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported layout mode: {layout_mode}")

        # Filter points
        if layout_mode not in ["fractal", "chaotic"]:
            for x, y in points:
                point = Point(x, y)
                if not utm_polygon.contains(point):
                    continue
                if dem_dataset and dsm_dataset:
                    suitable, reason = is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer_to_wgs84)
                    if not suitable:
                        print(f"[DEBUG] Rejected point ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}): {reason}")
                        continue
                too_close = False
                for existing in gcp_points:
                    dist = np.sqrt((x - existing['x'])**2 + (y - existing['y'])**2)
                    if dist < fam_spacing:
                        too_close = True
                        break
                if not too_close:
                    lon, lat = transformer_to_wgs84.transform(x, y)
                    pattern_score = unified_detection(len(gcp_points), 0)
                    gcp_points.append({"lat": lat, "lon": lon, "x": x, "y": y, "easting": x, "northing": y, "pattern_score": pattern_score})

        # Ensure minimum 10 GCPs
        if len(gcp_points) < 10:
            print(f"[WARNING] Only {len(gcp_points)} GCPs, adding random points")
            attempts = 0
            max_attempts = 100
            while len(gcp_points) < 10 and attempts < max_attempts:
                x = np.random.uniform(minx, maxx)
                y = np.random.uniform(miny, maxy)
                point = Point(x, y)
                if not utm_polygon.contains(point):
                    continue
                if dem_dataset and dsm_dataset:
                    suitable, reason = is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer_to_wgs84)
                    if not suitable:
                        print(f"[DEBUG] Rejected random point ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}): {reason}")
                        continue
                too_close = False
                for existing in gcp_points:
                    dist = np.sqrt((x - existing['x'])**2 + (y - existing['y'])**2)
                    if dist < fam_spacing:
                        too_close = True
                        break
                if not too_close:
                    lon, lat = transformer_to_wgs84.transform(x, y)
                    pattern_score = unified_detection(len(gcp_points), 0)
                    gcp_points.append({"lat": lat, "lon": lon, "x": x, "y": y, "easting": x, "northing": y, "pattern_score": pattern_score})
                attempts += 1

        # Filter using reject_coords_too_close
        gcp_points, _ = reject_coords_too_close(gcp_points, min_distance=fam_spacing, area_acres=area_acres)

        # Generate verification points
        verification_points = []
        offset_meters = fam_spacing * 0.5
        x_ver = np.arange(minx + offset_meters, maxx, fam_spacing)
        y_ver = np.arange(miny + offset_meters, maxy, fam_spacing)
        if len(x_ver) > 0 and len(y_ver) > 0:
            xv_ver, yv_ver = np.meshgrid(x_ver, y_ver)
            ver_points = np.vstack((xv_ver.ravel(), yv_ver.ravel())).T
            for x, y in ver_points:
                point = Point(x, y)
                if not utm_polygon.contains(point):
                    continue
                if dem_dataset and dsm_dataset:
                    suitable, reason = is_suitable_location(x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, transformer_to_wgs84)
                    if not suitable:
                        print(f"[DEBUG] Rejected verification point ({x:.2f}, {y:.2f}): {reason}")
                        continue
                too_close = False
                for existing in verification_points:
                    dist = np.sqrt((x - existing['x'])**2 + (y - existing['y'])**2)
                    if dist < fam_spacing:
                        too_close = True
                        break
                if not too_close:
                    lon, lat = transformer_to_wgs84.transform(x, y)
                    pattern_score = unified_detection(len(verification_points), 0)
                    verification_points.append({"lat": lat, "lon": lon, "x": x, "y": y, "easting": x, "northing": y, "pattern_score": pattern_score})

        verification_points, _ = reject_coords_too_close(verification_points, min_distance=fam_spacing, area_acres=area_acres)

        # Log results
        print(f"[DEBUG] Generated {len(gcp_points)} GCPs, {len(verification_points)} verification points")
        if gcp_points:
            print(f"[DEBUG] First 5 GCPs: {[{'lat': p['lat'], 'lon': p['lon'], 'pattern_score': p['pattern_score']} for p in gcp_points[:5]]}")
        if verification_points:
            print(f"[DEBUG] First 5 verification points: {[{'lat': p['lat'], 'lon': p['lon'], 'pattern_score': p['pattern_score']} for p in verification_points[:5]]}")
        if len(gcp_points) > 1:
            dist = np.sqrt((gcp_points[0]['x'] - gcp_points[1]['x'])**2 + (gcp_points[0]['y'] - gcp_points[1]['y'])**2)
            print(f"[DEBUG] Distance between first two GCPs: {dist:.2f}m")

        gcp_points = [{"lat": p["lat"], "lon": p["lon"], "pattern_score": p["pattern_score"]} for p in gcp_points]
        verification_points = [{"lat": p["lat"], "lon": p["lon"], "pattern_score": p["pattern_score"]} for p in verification_points]
        return gcp_points, verification_points
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] GCP generation failed: {e}")
        raise
    finally:
        if 'dem_dataset' in locals() and dem_dataset:
            dem_dataset.close()
        if 'dsm_dataset' in locals() and dsm_dataset:
            dsm_dataset.close()

def generate_verification_points(polygon_coords, gcp_points, spacing, flight_params=None, dem_path=None, dsm_path=None):
    """Generate verification points."""
    print(f"[DEBUG] Generating verification points with spacing={spacing}")
    try:
        _, verification_points = generate_gcps_within_polygon(
            polygon_coords, spacing, "grid", flight_params, dem_path, dsm_path
        )
        return verification_points
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[ERROR] Verification point generation failed: {e}")
        raise

Analysis of gcp_generator.py (Older Version)
Strengths of the Older Version:

FAM-Based Spacing: Uses calculate_fam_spacing with Fibonacci scaling based on area, ensuring adaptive point placement.
Terrain Filtering: Integrates is_suitable_location to filter points based on vegetation height (DSM-DEM > 2m) and water bodies, improving point suitability.
Multiple Layout Modes: Supports grid, triangular, diamond, spiral, fibonacci, fractal, and chaotic layouts, providing flexibility.
Minimum GCP Enforcement: Adds random points if fewer than 10 GCPs are generated, ensuring sufficient coverage.
Coordinate Transformation: Handles UTM (EPSG:32614) to WGS84 conversions, though hardcoded.
Integration with Flight Parameters: Uses compute_flight_parameters to adjust spacing dynamically.
Issues in the Older Version:

Hardcoded CRS: Uses EPSG:32614 in generate_gcps_within_polygon, causing misalignment for areas like the log’s (-82.638784, 39.986746) (Zone 17N, EPSG:32617).
Points Outside DSM Bounds: Hardcoded CRS likely caused points like (1204896.11, -10422451.65) to be outside DSM bounds due to incorrect transformations.
Complexity Scores: unified_detection may produce negative scores, contributing to the log’s -0.00.
Logging: Uses print instead of logging with %(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s.
Point Structure: Outputs minimal point dictionaries (lat, lon, pattern_score), lacking name, elevation, status, reason required by main_logic.py.
Rasterio Warning: is_suitable_location uses rowcol and sample, which may trigger rasterio.transform.py warnings if coordinates are invalid.
Performance: Repeated rasterio opens and inefficient point filtering.
Why It Worked Well:

Adaptive spacing via calculate_fam_spacing ensured appropriate point density.
Terrain filtering reduced unsuitable points, improving survey quality.
Multiple layout modes supported diverse use cases.
Minimum GCP enforcement prevented under-generation.
Why Recent Revisions May Have Broken It:

Simplified point structure may have caused compatibility issues with modern_ui.py’s PointEditorDialog.
Removed terrain filtering or reduced layout modes in some revisions.
Lack of bounds checking exacerbated DSM bounds issues.
Key Issues and Objectives
From the log and provided files:

Hardcoded UTM Zones: gcp_generator.py (EPSG:32614), main_logic.py (EPSG:32617), area_utils.py (EPSG:32614), dsm_manager.py (EPSG:32617), overlay_generator.py (EPSG:3857). All must use get_utm_zone.
Elevation Profile Bug: Log’s min=0.00, max=0.00, mean=0.00 from elevation_service.py’s get_srtm_elevation_bulk or main_logic.py’s max_vegetation_height.
Points Outside DSM Bounds: Caused by incorrect transformations in gcp_generator.py or dsm_manager.py.
Rasterio Warning: RuntimeWarning: invalid value encountered in cast from invalid coordinates in dsm_manager.py or gcp_generator.py.
Performance: Repeated rasterio opens; API retries in elevation_service.py.
Complexity Scores: Uniform -0.00 scores from unnormalized unified_detection or detect_elevation_cycles.
Logging: gcp_generator.py uses print instead of logging.
Math Tool Box: math_tool_box.py is primary; mathtoolbox_complete.py is legacy.
Redundant Files: overlay_map.py is a wrapper; uas_survey_tool.py duplicates modern_ui.py.
Installer: UAS_Survey_Tool_Installer.iss references icon.ico instead of app_icon.ico.
UI/UX Preferences: Retain modern_ui.py’s theme (#1e2a44, #3f5ca8), spacing (10–20px), and PointEditorDialog with rejected points added.

did modern_ui truncate part 2? here is revised main_logic:   import logging
from typing import List, Tuple, Dict
import numpy as np
from shapely.geometry import shape, Polygon, Point
from fastkml import kml
import rasterio
from simplekml import Kml
import zipfile


class MainLogic:
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger("MainLogic")
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
        self.polygon_utm: Polygon = None
        self.gcp_points: List[Tuple[float, float]] = []
        self.verification_points: List[Tuple[float, float]] = []
        self.polygon_area_acres: float = 0.0
        self.elevation_data: Dict = {'variance': 1.0}

    def load_kmz(self, kmz_path: str) -> bool:
        try:
            with zipfile.ZipFile(kmz_path, 'r') as kmz:
                with kmz.open('doc.kml', 'r') as kml_file:
                    kml_bytes = kml_file.read()

            k = kml.KML()
            k.from_string(kml_bytes)

            def get_features(obj):
                if hasattr(obj, 'features'):
                    attr = obj.features
                    if callable(attr):
                        return list(attr())
                    elif isinstance(attr, list):
                        return attr
                return []

            def find_polygon_feature(features):
                for feature in features:
                    sub_features = get_features(feature)
                    if hasattr(feature, 'geometry') and feature.geometry:
                        geom = shape(feature.geometry)
                        if geom.geom_type in ['Polygon', 'MultiPolygon']:
                            return geom
                    if sub_features:
                        geom = find_polygon_feature(sub_features)
                        if geom:
                            return geom
                return None

            polygon_geom = find_polygon_feature(get_features(k))

            if polygon_geom:
                self.polygon_utm = polygon_geom
                self.polygon_area_acres = polygon_geom.area * 0.000247105
                self.logger.info(f"Loaded polygon from KMZ with area {self.polygon_area_acres:.2f} acres")
                return True
            else:
                self.logger.error("No polygon geometry found in KMZ")
                return False

        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to load KMZ: {e}")
            return False

    def run_core_analysis(self) -> bool:
        self.logger.info("Starting core analysis...")
        if not self.polygon_utm:
            self.logger.error("Polygon must be loaded before analysis")
            return False
        try:
            dem_path = "path_to_dem.tif"
            dsm_path = "path_to_dsm.tif"
            max_veg = self.max_vegetation_height(dsm_path, dem_path)
            success = self.generate_gcp_plan(dsm_path=dsm_path, dem_path=dem_path)
            if not success:
                self.logger.error("GCP plan generation failed")
                return False
            self.logger.info("Core analysis completed successfully")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Core analysis failed: {e}")
            return False

    def generate_gcp_plan(self, dsm_path: str = None, dem_path: str = None) -> bool:
        try:
            if not self.polygon_utm:
                self.logger.error("Polygon must be loaded before generating GCP plan")
                return False

            min_gcp_count = 20
            min_ver_count = 30
            max_gcp_count = 120
            max_ver_count = 130

            area_factor_gcp = self.polygon_area_acres * 0.05
            area_factor_ver = self.polygon_area_acres * 0.1

            pattern_score = abs(self.unified_detection(len(self.gcp_points) if self.gcp_points else min_gcp_count, 0))
            elevation_variance = self.elevation_data.get('variance', 1.0)

            desired_gcp_count = int(min(max_gcp_count, max(min_gcp_count, area_factor_gcp * (1 + pattern_score + elevation_variance))))
            desired_ver_count = int(min(max_ver_count, max(min_ver_count, area_factor_ver * (1 + pattern_score + elevation_variance))))

            self.logger.info(f"Desired GCP count: {desired_gcp_count}, Verification count: {desired_ver_count}")

            self.gcp_points = generate_points_in_polygon(self.polygon_utm, desired_gcp_count)
            self.verification_points = generate_points_in_polygon(self.polygon_utm, desired_ver_count)

            if dsm_path and dem_path:
                with rasterio.open(dsm_path) as dsm_dataset, rasterio.open(dem_path) as dem_dataset:
                    max_veg_height = self.max_vegetation_height(dsm_path, dem_path)
                    self.gcp_points = [pt for pt in self.gcp_points if self.is_suitable_location(pt[0], pt[1], dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, None, max_veg_height)[0]]
                    self.verification_points = [pt for pt in self.verification_points if self.is_suitable_location(pt[0], pt[1], dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, None, max_veg_height)[0]]

            self.gcp_points = reject_coords_too_close(self.gcp_points, min_distance=15)
            self.verification_points = reject_coords_too_close(self.verification_points, min_distance=15)

            self.logger.info(f"Final GCP count after filtering: {len(self.gcp_points)}")
            self.logger.info(f"Final Verification count after filtering: {len(self.verification_points)}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"GCP plan generation failed: {e}")
            return False

    def export_kmz(self, output_path: str) -> bool:
        try:
            kml_doc = Kml()
            gcp_folder = kml_doc.newfolder(name="Ground Control Points (GCP)")
            for idx, (easting, northing) in enumerate(self.gcp_points, start=1):
                point = gcp_folder.newpoint(name=f"GCP-{idx}", coords=[(easting, northing)])
                point.style.iconstyle.icon.href = 'http://maps.google.com/mapfiles/kml/shapes/placemark_circle.png'
            ver_folder = kml_doc.newfolder(name="Verification Points (VCP)")
            for idx, (easting, northing) in enumerate(self.verification_points, start=1):
                point = ver_folder.newpoint(name=f"VCP-{idx}", coords=[(easting, northing)])
                point.style.iconstyle.icon.href = 'http://maps.google.com/mapfiles/kml/shapes/target.png'
            kml_doc.savekmz(output_path)
            self.logger.info(f"Exported KMZ to {output_path}")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"KMZ export failed: {e}")
            return False

    def unified_detection(self, val1, val2) -> float:
        return 0.5

    def max_vegetation_height(self, dsm_path, dem_path) -> float:
        return 10.0

    def is_suitable_location(self, x, y, dem_dataset, dsm_dataset, other, max_veg_height):
        return (True, "Suitable")


# --- Utility Functions ---

def generate_points_in_polygon(polygon: Polygon, num_points: int) -> List[Tuple[float, float]]:
    points = []
    minx, miny, maxx, maxy = polygon.bounds
    attempts = 0
    max_attempts = num_points * 10
    while len(points) < num_points and attempts < max_attempts:
        x = np.random.uniform(minx, maxx)
        y = np.random.uniform(miny, maxy)
        pt = Point(x, y)
        if polygon.contains(pt):
            points.append((x, y))
        attempts += 1
    return points

def reject_coords_too_close(points: List[Tuple[float, float]], min_distance: float) -> List[Tuple[float, float]]:
    filtered_points = []
    for pt in points:
        if all(np.linalg.norm(np.array(pt) - np.array(existing)) >= min_distance for existing in filtered_points):
            filtered_points.append(pt)
    return filtered_points
